the Atlantic hurricane of 2017.         <a href="/wiki/Guadeloupe" title="Guadeloupe">\n           Guadeloupe\n          </a>\n          , and the\n          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/U.S._Virgin_Islands" title="U.S. Virgin Islands">\n           U.S. Virgin Islands\n          </a>\n          )\n         </small>\n         ,\n         <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico" title="Puerto Rico">\n          Puerto Rico\n         </a>\n         ,\n         <a href="/wiki/Dominican_Republic" title="Dominican Republic">\n          Dominican Republic\n         </a>\n         ,\n         <a href="/wiki/Haiti" title="Haiti">\n          Haiti\n         </a>\n         ,\n         <a href="/wiki/Turks_and_Caicos_Islands" title="Turks and Caicos Islands">\n          Turks and Caicos Islands\n         </a>\n         ,\n         <a Southeastern United States\n         </a>\n         ,\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mid-Atlantic_States" title="Mid-Atlantic States">\n          Mid-Atlantic States\n         </a>\n         ,\n         <a href="/wiki/Ireland" title="Ireland">\n          Ireland\n         </a>\n         ,\n         <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">\n          United Kingdom\n         </a>\n         ,\n         <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">\n          France\n         </a>\n         ,\n         <a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain">\n          Spain\n         </a>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;padding:0px 2px">\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center; border-top:#aaa 1px solid;">\n         Part of the\n         <b>\n          <a href="/wiki/2017_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2017 Atlantic hurricane season">\n           2017 Atlantic hurricane season\n          </a>\n         </b>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr style="display:none">\n        <td colspan="2">\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       <b>\n        Hurricane Maria\n       </b>\n       is regarded as the worst natural disaster on record in\n       <a href="/wiki/Dominica" title="Dominica">\n        Dominica\n       </a>\n       , and caused catastrophic damage and a major\n       <a href="/wiki/Humanitarian_crisis" title="Humanitarian crisis">\n        humanitarian crisis\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico" title="Puerto Rico">\n        Puerto Rico\n       </a>\n       . The\n       <a href="/wiki/List_of_the_most_intense_tropical_cyclones#North_Atlantic_Ocean" title="List of the most intense tropical cyclones">\n        tenth-most intense Atlantic hurricane\n       </a>\n       on record, Maria was the thirteenth\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone_naming" title="Tropical cyclone naming">\n        named storm\n       </a>\n       , seventh consecutive\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hurricane" title="Hurricane">\n        hurricane\n       </a>\n       , fourth\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Major_hurricane" title="Major hurricane">\n        major hurricane\n       </a>\n       , and the second\n       <a href="/wiki/List_of_Category_5_Atlantic_hurricanes" title="List of Category 5 Atlantic hurricanes">\n        Category\xc2\xa05 hurricane\n       </a>\n       of the hyperactive\n       <a href="/wiki/2017_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2017 Atlantic hurricane season">\n        2017 Atlantic hurricane season\n       </a>\n       . At its peak, the hurricane caused catastrophic damage and numerous fatalities across the northeastern\n       <a href="/wiki/Caribbean" title="Caribbean">\n        Caribbean\n       </a>\n       , compounding recovery efforts in the areas of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Leeward_Islands" title="Leeward Islands">\n        Leeward Islands\n       </a>\n       already struck by\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Irma" title="Hurricane Irma">\n        Hurricane Irma\n       </a>\n       just two weeks prior. Maria was the third consecutive major hurricane to threaten the Leeward Islands in two weeks, after Irma made landfall in several of the islands two weeks prior and\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Jose_(2017)" title="Hurricane Jose (2017)">\n        Hurricane Jose\n       </a>\n       passed dangerously close bringing tropical storm force winds to\n       <a href="/wiki/Barbuda" title="Barbuda">\n        Barbuda\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Originating from a\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_wave" title="Tropical wave">\n        tropical wave\n       </a>\n       , Maria became a tropical storm on September 16, east of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Lesser_Antilles" title="Lesser Antilles">\n        Lesser Antilles\n       </a>\n       . Highly favorable\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone#Factors" title="Tropical cyclone">\n        environmental conditions\n       </a>\n       allowed the storm to undergo\n       <a href="/wiki/Rapid_intensification" title="Rapid intensification">\n        explosive intensification\n       </a>\n       as it approached the island arc. The hurricane reached Category\xc2\xa05 strength on September 18 upon making landfall on Dominica, producing extreme winds across the entire island. Afterwards, Maria achieved its peak intensity over the eastern Caribbean with\n       <a href="/wiki/Maximum_sustained_wind" title="Maximum sustained wind">\n        maximum sustained winds\n       </a>\n       of 175\xc2\xa0mph (280\xc2\xa0km/h) and a pressure of 908\xc2\xa0mbar (hPa; 26.81\xc2\xa0inHg), making it the tenth-most intense Atlantic hurricane on record. Weakening slightly, but retaining its ferocious winds, Maria struck Puerto Rico as a high-end Category\xc2\xa04 hurricane on September 20. Interaction with land weakened the hurricane, though it regained some strength as it moved northeast of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bahamas" title="Bahamas">\n        The Bahamas\n       </a>\n       . Moving slowly to the north, Maria gradually degraded and weakened to a tropical storm on September 28. Embedded in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Westerlies" title="Westerlies">\n        westerlies\n       </a>\n       , Maria accelerated toward the east and later east-northeast over the open Atlantic, becoming\n       <a href="/wiki/Extratropical_cyclone" title="Extratropical cyclone">\n        extratropical\n       </a>\n       on September 30 and dissipating by October 3.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       As of November 3, at least 98\xc2\xa0people are confirmed to have been killed by the hurricane: 54 in Puerto Rico, 28 in Dominica, 5 in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Dominican_Republic" title="Dominican Republic">\n        Dominican Republic\n       </a>\n       , 4 in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Contiguous_United_States" title="Contiguous United States">\n        contiguous United States\n       </a>\n       , 3 in\n       <a href="/wiki/Haiti" title="Haiti">\n        Haiti\n       </a>\n       , 2 in\n       <a href="/wiki/Guadeloupe" title="Guadeloupe">\n        Guadeloupe\n       </a>\n       , and 1 in the\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Virgin_Islands" title="United States Virgin Islands">\n        United States Virgin Islands\n       </a>\n       . Hundreds of others, mostly in Dominica and Puerto Rico, are still missing. San Juan Mayor Yul\xc3\xadn Cruz claimed that the actual death toll in Puerto Rico may actually be as high as 500.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-10_times_higher_1-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-10_times_higher-1">\n         [1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Maria wrought catastrophic damage to the entirety of Dominica, which suffered an island-wide communication blackout. Much of the housing stock and infrastructure were left beyond repair, while the island\'s lush vegetation had been practically eradicated. The islands of Guadeloupe and\n       <a href="/wiki/Martinique" title="Martinique">\n        Martinique\n       </a>\n       endured widespread flooding, damaged roofs and uprooted trees. Puerto Rico suffered catastrophic damage, including destruction of its previously damaged electrical grid. For weeks in Maria\'s wake, most of the island\'s population suffered from flooding and lack of resources, compounded by the slow relief process. Total losses from the hurricane are estimated at between $15.9 and $95 billion (2017\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/USD" title="USD">\n        USD\n       </a>\n       ), mostly in Puerto Rico, making Maria\'s cost comparable to that of previous Hurricanes Irma and\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Harvey" title="Hurricane Harvey">\n        Harvey\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-consumerinfoline_2-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-consumerinfoline-2">\n         [2]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-insuredlosses_3-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-insuredlosses-3">\n         [3]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-MariaDamageEstimate_4-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-MariaDamageEstimate-4">\n         [4]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-95_billion_storm_5-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-95_billion_storm-5">\n         [5]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n      </p>\n      <div class="toc" id="toc">\n       <div class="toctitle">\n        <h2>\n         Contents\n        </h2>\n       </div>\n       <ul>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-1">\n         <a href="#Meteorological_history">\n          <span class="tocnumber">\n           1\n          </span>\n          <span class="toctext">\n           Meteorological history\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </li>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-2">\n         <a href="#Preparations">\n          <span class="tocnumber">\n           2\n          </span>\n          <span class="toctext">\n           Preparations\n          </span>\n         </a>\n         <ul>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-3">\n           <a href="#Puerto_Rico">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             2.1\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             Puerto Rico\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-4">\n           <a href="#Mainland_United_States">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             2.2\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             Mainland United States\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n         </ul>\n        </li>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-5">\n         <a href="#Impact_in_the_Lesser_Antilles">\n          <span class="tocnumber">\n           3\n          </span>\n          <span class="toctext">\n           Impact in the Lesser Antilles\n          </span>\n         </a>\n         <ul>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-6">\n           <a href="#Windward_Islands">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             3.1\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             Windward Islands\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-7">\n           <a href="#Dominica">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             3.2\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             Dominica\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-8">\n           <a href="#Guadeloupe">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             3.3\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             Guadeloupe\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-9">\n           <a href="#United_States_Virgin_Islands">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             3.4\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             United States Virgin Islands\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n         </ul>\n        </li>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-10">\n         <a href="#Impact_in_the_Greater_Antilles_and_the_United_States">\n          <span class="tocnumber">\n           4\n          </span>\n          <span class="toctext">\n           Impact in the Greater Antilles and the United States\n          </span>\n         </a>\n         <ul>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-11">\n           <a href="#Puerto_Rico_2">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             4.1\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             Puerto Rico\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-12">\n           <a href="#Hispaniola">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             4.2\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n class="tocnumber">\n             4.3\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             Mainland United States\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n         </ul>\n        </li>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-14">\n         <a href="#Aftermath">\n          <span class="tocnumber">\n           5\n          </span>\n          <span class="toctext">\n           Aftermath\n          </span>\n         </a>\n         <ul>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-15">\n           <a href="#Dominica_2">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             5.1\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             Dominica\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-16">\n           <a href="#Puerto_Rico_3">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             5.2\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             Puerto Rico\n            </span>\n           </a>\n           <ul>\n            <li class="toclevel-3 tocsection-17">\n             <a href="#Possible_leptospirosis_outbreak">\n              <span class="tocnumber">\n               5.2.1\n              </span>\n              <span class="toctext">\n               Possible leptospirosis outbreak\n              </span>\n             </a>\n            </li>\n            <li class="toclevel-3 tocsection-18">\n             <a href="#Additional_fatalities">\n              <span class="tocnumber">\n               5.2.2\n              </span>\n              <span class="toctext">\n               Additional fatalities\n              </span>\n             </a>\n            </li>\n            <li class="toclevel-3 tocsection-19">\n             <a href="#Whitefish_Energy">\n              <span class="tocnumber">\n               5.2.3\n              </span>\n              <span class="toctext">\n               Whitefish Energy\n              </span>\n             </a>\n            </li>\n           </ul>\n          </li>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-20">\n           <a href="#U.S._Virgin_Islands">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             5.3\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             U.S. Virgin Islands\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-21">\n           <a href="#Criticism_of_U.S._government_response">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             5.4\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n           References\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </li>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-24">\n         <a href="#External_links">\n          <span <p>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Meteorological_history">\n        Meteorological history\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Maria&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Meteorological history">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Maria_2017_track.png">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2290" data-file-width="3000" height="229" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1d/Maria_2017_track.png/300px-Maria_2017_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1d/Maria_2017_track.png/450px-Maria_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1d/Maria_2017_track.png/600px-Maria_2017_track.png 2x" width="300"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Maria_2017_track.png" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Map plotting the track and intensity of the storm, according to the\n         <a href="/wiki/Saffir%E2%80%93Simpson_scale" title="Saffir\xe2\x80\x93Simpson scale">\n          Saffir\xe2\x80\x93Simpson scale\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/National_Hurricane_Center" title="National Hurricane Center">\n        National Hurricane Center\n       </a>\n       (NHC) began monitoring two\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_wave" title="Tropical wave">\n        tropical waves\n       </a>\n       on September 13.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6">\n        <a href="#cite_note-6">\n         [6]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The easternmost wave quickly spun up into what would become\n       <a href="/wiki/2017_Atlantic_hurricane_season#Hurricane_Lee" title="2017 Atlantic hurricane season">\n        Hurricane Lee\n       </a>\n       , while the western one continued moving generally westward. With generally favorable conditions in the disturbance\'s path, development into a tropical cyclone seemed likely.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7">\n        <a href="#cite_note-7">\n         [7]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       During those two days the disturbance became better organized,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8">\n        <a href="#cite_note-8">\n         [8]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and by September 16,\n       <a href="/wiki/Rainband" title="Rainband">\n        convective banding\n       </a>\n       became established around a poorly organized circulation. As the system was an imminent threat to land despite the center not being well-defined, the NHC initiated advisories on it as "Potential Tropical Cyclone Fifteen" at 15:00\xc2\xa0UTC, in accordance with a policy change enacted at the start of the season.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-D1_9-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-D1-9">\n         [9]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-10">\n        <a href="#cite_note-10">\n         [10]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       A mid-level\n       <a href="/wiki/Ridge_(meteorology)" title="Ridge (meteorology)">\n        ridge\n       </a>\n       anchored north of the disturbance steered it generally west-northwest into a region highly favorable for\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclogenesis" title="Tropical cyclogenesis">\n        further development\n       </a>\n       .\n       <a href="/wiki/Sea_surface_temperature" title="Sea surface temperature">\n        Sea surface temperatures\n       </a>\n       of 84\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0F (29\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0C), low\n       <a href="/wiki/Wind_shear" title="Wind shear">\n        wind shear\n       </a>\n       , and ample moisture were anticipated to foster strengthening to hurricane-status before the system reached the\n       <a href="/wiki/Lesser_Antilles" title="Lesser Antilles">\n        Lesser Antilles\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-D1_9-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-D1-9">\n         [9]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-D4_11-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-D4-11">\n         [11]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       As the disturbance continued to grow increasingly well-defined throughout the day, it was later upgraded to a moderate-range tropical storm \xe2\x80\x93 based on satellite estimates \xe2\x80\x93 at 21:00\xc2\xa0UTC that day,\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone_naming" title="Tropical cyclone naming">\n        receiving the name\n       </a>\n       <i>\n        Maria\n       </i>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12">\n        <a href="#cite_note-12">\n         [12]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       At that time, Maria was situated 620\xc2\xa0mi (1,000\xc2\xa0km) east-southeast of the Lesser Antilles.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13">\n        <a href="#cite_note-13">\n         [13]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <table align="right" border="1" class="wikitable" style="font-size: 92%;">\n       <tr>\n        <th colspan="6" style="background:#ccf;">\n         <a href="/wiki/List_of_the_most_intense_tropical_cyclones#Atlantic_Ocean" title="List of the most intense tropical cyclones">\n          Most intense Atlantic hurricanes\n         </a>\n        </th>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th rowspan="2">\n         Rank\n        </th>\n        <th rowspan="2">\n         Hurricane\n        </th>\n        <th rowspan="2">\n         Season\n        </th>\n        <th colspan="2">\n         Pressure\n        </th>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         882\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         26.05\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         2\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Gilbert" title="Hurricane Gilbert">\n          Gilbert\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/1988_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="1988 Atlantic hurricane season">\n          1988\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         888\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         26.23\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         3\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/1935_Labor_Day_hurricane" title="1935 Labor Day hurricane">\n          "Labor Day"\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/1935_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="1935 Atlantic hurricane season">\n          1935\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         892\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         26.34\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         4\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Rita" title="Hurricane Rita">\n          Rita\n 895\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         26.43\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         5\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Allen" title="Hurricane Allen">\n          Allen\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/1980_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="1980 Atlantic hurricane season">\n          1980\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         899\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         26.55\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         6\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Camille" title="Hurricane Camille">\n          Camille\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/1969_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="1969 Atlantic hurricane season">\n          1969\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         900\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         26.58\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         7\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Katrina" title="Hurricane Katrina">\n          Katrina\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/2005_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2005 Atlantic hurricane season">\n          2005\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         902\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         26.64\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th rowspan="2">\n         8\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Mitch" title="Hurricane Mitch">\n          Mitch\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/1998_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="1998 Atlantic hurricane season">\n          1998\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td rowspan="2">\n         905\n        </td>\n        <td rowspan="2">\n         26.73\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Dean" title="Hurricane Dean">\n          Dean\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/2007_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2007 Atlantic hurricane season">\n          2007\n         </a>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         10\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         <a class="mw-selflink selflink">\n          Maria\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/2017_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2017 Atlantic hurricane season">\n          2017\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         908\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         26.81\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr class="small">\n        <th colspan="6">\n         Source: HURDAT\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-HURDAT_14-0">\n          <a href="#cite_note-HURDAT-14">\n           [14]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </th>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       A\n       <a href="/wiki/Central_dense_overcast" title="Central dense overcast">\n        central dense overcast\n       </a>\n       and favorable\n       <a href="/wiki/Outflow_(meteorology)" title="Outflow (meteorology)">\n        outflow\n       </a>\n       developed atop the center of circulation, which enabled Maria to become further organized throughout the early morning hours of September 17.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-D4_11-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-D4-11">\n         [11]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       After a brief intrusion of dry air exposed the circulation,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-15">\n        <a href="#cite_note-15">\n         [15]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       a convective burst occurred over the center and intensification resumed.\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hurricane_Hunters" title="Hurricane Hunters">\n        Hurricane Hunters\n       </a>\n       investigating the system observed surface winds of 74\xc2\xa0mph (119\xc2\xa0km/h) and a formative\n       <a href="/wiki/Eye_(cyclone)" title="Eye (cyclone)">\n        eye\n       </a>\n       feature. Accordingly, the NHC upgraded Maria to hurricane status at 21:00\xc2\xa0UTC.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-16">\n        <a href="#cite_note-16">\n         [16]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Expansion of the central dense overcast and an increasingly complete eyewall signaled steady intensification throughout the overnight of September\xc2\xa017\xe2\x80\x9318.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-17">\n        <a href="#cite_note-17">\n         [17]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Considerable\n       <a href="/wiki/Lightning" title="Lightning">\n        lightning\n       </a>\n       activity was identified within the hurricane\'s core early on September 18 and statistical models indicated a high probability of\n       <a href="/wiki/Rapid_intensification" title="Rapid intensification">\n        rapid intensification\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18">\n        <a href="#cite_note-18">\n         [18]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Explosive strengthening took place shortly thereafter, with aircraft reconnaissance finding surface winds of 120\xc2\xa0mph (195\xc2\xa0km/h) and a central pressure of 959\xc2\xa0mbar (hPa; 28.32\xc2\xa0inHg), making Maria a Category\xc2\xa03 hurricane on the\n       <a href="/wiki/Saffir%E2%80%93Simpson_scale" title="Saffir\xe2\x80\x93Simpson scale">\n        Saffir\xe2\x80\x93Simpson scale\n       </a>\n       , and hence a major hurricane. Additionally, radar data revealed a well-defined 12\xc2\xa0mi (19\xc2\xa0km) wide eye.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-19">\n        <a href="#cite_note-19">\n         [19]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The eye contracted slightly to 9\xc2\xa0mi (14\xc2\xa0km) as intensification continued, and the system reached Category\xc2\xa04 strength by 21:00\xc2\xa0UTC.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-20">\n        <a href="#cite_note-20">\n         [20]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Composite_Reflectivity_San_Juan_radar_92017.png">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="616" data-file-width="693" height="196" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/67/Composite_Reflectivity_San_Juan_radar_92017.png/220px-Composite_Reflectivity_San_Juan_radar_92017.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/67/Composite_Reflectivity_San_Juan_radar_92017.png/330px-Composite_Reflectivity_San_Juan_radar_92017.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/67/Composite_Reflectivity_San_Juan_radar_92017.png/440px-Composite_Reflectivity_San_Juan_radar_92017.png 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Composite_Reflectivity_San_Juan_radar_92017.png" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Radar imagery of Hurricane Maria from Puerto Rico at 09:36\xc2\xa0UTC (5:36\xc2\xa0a.m. local time), shortly before it stopped transmitting data.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Rapid intensification culminated late on September 18, with Maria achieving Category\xc2\xa05 status just 15\xc2\xa0mi (25\xc2\xa0km) east-southeast of Dominica.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-21">\n        <a href="#cite_note-21">\n         [21]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Hurricane Hunters observed surface winds of 160\xc2\xa0mph (260\xc2\xa0km/h) and a pressure of 925\xc2\xa0mbar (hPa; 27.32\xc2\xa0inHg) at this time.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-22">\n        <a href="#cite_note-22">\n         [22]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Maria made\n       <a href="/wiki/Landfall" title="Landfall">\n        landfall\n       </a>\n       in Dominica at 01:15\xc2\xa0UTC on September 19,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Dominica_landfall_TCU_23-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Dominica_landfall_TCU-23">\n         [23]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       becoming the first Category\xc2\xa05 hurricane on record to strike the island nation.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-24">\n        <a href="#cite_note-24">\n         [24]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Interaction with the mountains of Dominica imparted slight weakening of the hurricane to Category\xc2\xa04; however, once over the\n       <a href="/wiki/Caribbean_Sea" title="Caribbean Sea">\n        Caribbean Sea\n       </a>\n       Maria regained Category\xc2\xa05 intensity.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-25">\n        <a href="#cite_note-25">\n         [25]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-26">\n        <a href="#cite_note-26">\n         [26]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Additional strengthening took place as the storm tracked northwest toward\n       <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico" title="Puerto Rico">\n        Puerto Rico\n       </a>\n       . Despite the formation of concentric eyewalls\xe2\x80\x94the larger one spanning 25 to 35\xc2\xa0mi (40 to 56\xc2\xa0km) and the smaller only 5\xc2\xa0mi (8.0\xc2\xa0km), signalling the start of an\n       <a href="/wiki/Eyewall_replacement_cycle" title="Eyewall replacement cycle">\n        eyewall replacement cycle\n       </a>\n       \xe2\x80\x94the inner violent core remained undisrupted through the afternoon.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-27">\n        <a href="#cite_note-27">\n         [27]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Maria attained its peak intensity around 04:00\xc2\xa0UTC on September 20, roughly 30\xc2\xa0mi (45\xc2\xa0km) south of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/St._Croix" title="St. Croix">\n        St. Croix\n       </a>\n       . Sustained winds reached 175\xc2\xa0mph (280\xc2\xa0km/h) and its central pressure bottomed out at 908\xc2\xa0mbar (hPa; 26.85\xc2\xa0inHg); this ranks it as the tenth-most intense Atlantic hurricane since reliable records began.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-28">\n        <a href="#cite_note-28">\n         [28]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-29">\n        <a href="#cite_note-29">\n         [29]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-30">\n        <a href="#cite_note-30">\n         [30]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Maria_GOES_Floater_Rainbow_IR_0925EDT_20-Sept-2017.gif">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="480" data-file-width="720" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ad/Maria_GOES_Floater_Rainbow_IR_0925EDT_20-Sept-2017.gif/220px-Maria_GOES_Floater_Rainbow_IR_0925EDT_20-Sept-2017.gif" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ad/Maria_GOES_Floater_Rainbow_IR_0925EDT_20-Sept-2017.gif/330px-Maria_GOES_Floater_Rainbow_IR_0925EDT_20-Sept-2017.gif 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ad/Maria_GOES_Floater_Rainbow_IR_0925EDT_20-Sept-2017.gif/440px-Maria_GOES_Floater_Rainbow_IR_0925EDT_20-Sept-2017.gif 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Maria_GOES_Floater_Rainbow_IR_0925EDT_20-Sept-2017.gif" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Infrared loop of Hurricane Maria passing St.\xc2\xa0Croix, Vieques, and landfalling on Puerto Rico on the morning of September 20\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The hurricane made its closest approach to St. Croix around 05:00\xc2\xa0UTC on September 20, passing within 20\xc2\xa0mi (30\xc2\xa0km) of the island; the storm\'s outer eyewall lashed the island while the more violent inner eye remained offshore.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-31">\n        <a href="#cite_note-31">\n         [31]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Hours later, around 08:00\xc2\xa0UTC, the outer eyewall struck\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Vieques" title="Vieques">\n        Vieques\n       </a>\n       , an island off the eastern coast of Puerto Rico.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-32">\n        <a href="#cite_note-32">\n         [32]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       By this time, the outer eye became dominant as the inner one decayed, and the eyewall replacement cycle caused Maria to weaken to Category\xc2\xa04 strength.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-33">\n        <a href="#cite_note-33">\n         [33]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Maria made landfall just south of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Yabucoa" title="Yabucoa">\n        Yabucoa\n       </a>\n       , Puerto Rico, around 10:15\xc2\xa0UTC with sustained winds of 155\xc2\xa0mph (250\xc2\xa0km/h),\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-34">\n        <a href="#cite_note-34">\n         [34]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       making it the strongest to hit the island since the\n       <a href="/wiki/1928_Okeechobee_hurricane" title="1928 Okeechobee hurricane">\n        1928 San Felipe Segundo hurricane\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-35">\n        <a href="#cite_note-35">\n         [35]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Maria maintained a general west-northwest course across Puerto Rico, emerging over the Atlantic Ocean shortly before 18:00\xc2\xa0UTC. Interaction with the mountainous terrain resulted in substantial weakening; sustained winds fell to 110\xc2\xa0mph (175\xc2\xa0km/h) and the central pressure rose to 957\xc2\xa0mbars (hPa; 28.26\xc2\xa0inHg).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-36">\n        <a href="#cite_note-36">\n         [36]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       With favorable environmental conditions, Maria steadily reorganized as it moved away from Puerto Rico. A large eye, 45\xc2\xa0mi (75\xc2\xa0km) wide, developed with deep convection blossoming around it. Early on September 21, the system regained Category\xc2\xa03 intensity.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-37">\n        <a href="#cite_note-37">\n         [37]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Initially, cooler waters\n       <a href="/wiki/Upwelling" title="Upwelling">\n        stirred up\n       </a>\n       by\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Irma" title="Hurricane Irma">\n        Hurricane Irma\n       </a>\n       two weeks prior limited Maria\'s reorganization.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-38">\n        <a href="#cite_note-38">\n         [38]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       During the afternoon of September 21, the system traversed the\n       <a href="/wiki/Navidad_Bank" title="Navidad Bank">\n        Navidad\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Silver_Bank" title="Silver Bank">\n        Silver\n       </a>\n       banks north of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Dominican_Republic" title="Dominican Republic">\n        Dominican Republic\n       </a>\n       ;\n       <a href="/wiki/Wave_shoaling" title="Wave shoaling">\n        shoaling\n       </a>\n       from the region\'s shallow waters temporarily interfered with measurements of surface winds.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-39">\n        <a href="#cite_note-39">\n         [39]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Convection around the storm\'s eye deepened and its eye became better defined that night, and the hurricane reached a tertiary peak with sustained winds of 125\xc2\xa0mph (205\xc2\xa0km/h).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-40">\n        <a href="#cite_note-40">\n         [40]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       An increase in southwesterly wind shear prompted gradual weakening of the hurricane, starting with restriction of banding features and later degradation of the eyewall.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-41">\n        <a href="#cite_note-41">\n         [41]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-42">\n        <a href="#cite_note-42">\n         [42]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Late on September 22, the hurricane turned north-northwest as it reached the western periphery of the ridge previously steering it northwest.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-43">\n        <a href="#cite_note-43">\n         [43]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Maria fluctuated in organization throughout September 23, with its eye periodically clearing and becoming cloud-filled; it maintained Category\xc2\xa03 hurricane strength during this phase.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-44">\n        <a href="#cite_note-44">\n         [44]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-45">\n        <a href="#cite_note-45">\n         [45]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Despite a decreasing central pressure, the storm finally weakened to Category\xc2\xa02 strength early on September 24. Hurricane Hunters observed flight-level winds of 116 to 135\xc2\xa0mph (187 to 217\xc2\xa0km/h); however, surface wind returns by the NOAA\'s\n       <a href="/wiki/Microwave_radiometer" title="Microwave radiometer">\n        Stepped-Frequency Microwave Radiometer\n       </a>\n       were only 90\xc2\xa0mph (150\xc2\xa0km/h). This indicated below-average mixing down of winds aloft.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-46">\n        <a href="#cite_note-46">\n         [46]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-D34_47-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-D34-47">\n         [47]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       By this time, Maria\'s trajectory shifted almost due north between the aforementioned ridge and a\n       <a href="/wiki/Block_(meteorology)#Cut-off_highs_and_lows" title="Block (meteorology)">\n        cut-off low\n       </a>\n       over the eastern\n       <a href="/wiki/Gulf_of_Mexico" title="Gulf of Mexico">\n        Gulf of Mexico\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-D34_47-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-D34-47">\n         [47]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Weakening accelerated later on September 24 into September 25, as the hurricane traversed a cold wake\xe2\x80\x94with sea surface temperatures of 75\xe2\x80\x9377\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0F (24\xe2\x80\x9325\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0C)\xe2\x80\x94created by\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Jose_(2017)" title="Hurricane Jose (2017)">\n        Hurricane Jose\n       </a>\n       a week prior. Maria degraded to Category\xc2\xa01 strength during this time.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-48">\n        <a href="#cite_note-48">\n         [48]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Early on September 25, Maria\'s structure changed dramatically as its inner-core collapsed. The low-level circulation became exposed to the northwest, and most of the deep convection shifted to the eastern half of the storm.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-49">\n        <a href="#cite_note-49">\n         [49]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Maria further weakened into a tropical storm during the late afternoon of September 26.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-50">\n        <a href="#cite_note-50">\n         [50]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       However, a sustained convective burst resulted in Maria\'s winds increasing to hurricane-force once again on September 27,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-51">\n        <a href="#cite_note-51">\n         [51]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       with banding features evident on the eastern part of the circulation.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-52">\n        <a href="#cite_note-52">\n         [52]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Despite this, northwesterly wind shear continued to impinge on the storm, and Maria once again weakened to a tropical storm early on September 28. Simultaneously, Maria began to accelerate to the east-northeast as it became embedded into the mid-latitude westerlies.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-53">\n        <a href="#cite_note-53">\n         [53]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Gradually weakening, Maria soon began to move over sea surface temperatures of 73\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0F (23\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0C) and below, causing most of its convection to dissipate. Late on September 30, Maria transitioned into an\n       <a href="/wiki/Extratropical_cyclone" title="Extratropical cyclone">\n        extratropical cyclone\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-54">\n        <a href="#cite_note-54">\n         [54]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       During the next couple of days, Maria\'s remnant accelerated towards the\n       <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">\n        United Kingdom\n       </a>\n       , while rapidly weakening.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-October_1_weather_map_55-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-October_1_weather_map-55">\n         [55]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-October_2_weather_map_56-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-October_2_weather_map-56">\n         [56]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Maria\'s remnants later crossed the\n       <a href="/wiki/Iberian_Peninsula" title="Iberian Peninsula">\n        Iberian Peninsula\n       </a>\n       into the western\n       <a href="/wiki/Mediterranean_Sea" title="Mediterranean Sea">\n        Mediterranean Sea\n       </a>\n       on October 3, before being absorbed by another frontal system later on the same day.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-October_3_weather_map_57-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-October_3_weather_map-57">\n         [57]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Preparations">\n        Preparations\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Maria&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Preparations">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <table class="plainlinks metadata ambox mbox-small-left ambox-content" role="presentation">\n       <tr>\n        <td class="mbox-image">\n         <a //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/40px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png 2x" width="20"/>\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td class="mbox-text">\n title="Play media">\n          <span class="play-btn-large">\n           <span class="mw-tmh-playtext">\n            Play media\n           </span>\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </div>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Navy_Helps_Evacuate_Military_From_U.S._Virgin_Islands_Ahead_of_Hurricane_Maria.webm" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         The U.S. Navy helps evacuate military personnel from the U.S. Virgin Islands, ahead of Hurricane Maria\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Upon the initiation of the\n       <a href="/wiki/National_Hurricane_Center" title="National Hurricane Center">\n        National Hurricane Center\n       </a>\n       (NHC)\'s first advisories for the system that would become Tropical Storm Maria on the morning of September 16, the government of\n       <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">\n        France\n       </a>\n       issued tropical storm watches for the islands of\n       <a href="/wiki/Martinique" title="Martinique">\n        Martinique\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Guadeloupe" title="Guadeloupe">\n        Guadeloupe\n       </a>\n       , while\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/St._Lucia" title="St. Lucia">\n        St. Lucia\n       </a>\n       issued a tropical storm watch for its citizens, and the government of\n       <a href="/wiki/Barbados" title="Barbados">\n        Barbados\n       </a>\n       issued a similar watch for\n       <a href="/wiki/Dominica" title="Dominica">\n        Dominica\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-public_advisory_1_58-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-public_advisory_1-58">\n         [58]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Barbados would later that day declare a tropical storm watch for its citizens and\n       <a href="/wiki/Saint_Vincent_and_the_Grenadines" title="Saint Vincent and the Grenadines">\n        Saint Vincent and the Grenadines\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-public_advisory_1a_59-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-public_advisory_1a-59">\n         [59]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The government of\n       <a href="/wiki/Antigua_and_Barbuda" title="Antigua and Barbuda">\n        Antigua and Barbuda\n       </a>\n       issued Hurricane watches for the islands of\n       <a href="/wiki/Antigua" title="Antigua">\n        Antigua\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Barbuda" title="Barbuda">\n        Barbuda\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/St._Kitts" title="St. Kitts">\n        St. Kitts\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Nevis" title="Nevis">\n        Nevis\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Montserrat" title="Montserrat">\n        Montserrat\n       </a>\n       by the time of the NHC\'s second advisory which declared Maria a tropical storm.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-public_advisory_2_60-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-public_advisory_2-60">\n         [60]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-washington_post_1_61-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-washington_post_1-61">\n         [61]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Dominican_Republic" title="Dominican Republic">\n        Dominican Republic\n       </a>\n       activated the\n       <a href="/wiki/International_Charter_on_Space_and_Major_Disasters" title="International Charter on Space and Major Disasters">\n        International Charter on Space and Major Disasters\n       </a>\n       for humanitarian satellite coverage on the 20th.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Dominican_Republic_Activates_the_International_Charter_on_Space_and_Major_Disasters_62-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Dominican_Republic_Activates_the_International_Charter_on_Space_and_Major_Disasters-62">\n         [62]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Puerto_Rico">\n        Puerto Rico\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Maria&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Puerto Rico">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Still recovering from Hurricane Irma two weeks prior, approximately 80,000\xc2\xa0remained without power as Maria approached.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-63">\n        <a href="#cite_note-63">\n         [63]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico_Electric_Power_Authority" title="Puerto Rico Electric Power Authority">\n        Puerto Rico Electric Power Authority\n       </a>\n       (PREPA) struggled with increasing debt, reaching $9\xc2\xa0billion even before the hurricanes prompting them to file for bankruptcy. Furthermore, the company lost 30\xc2\xa0percent of its employees since 2012. Aging infrastructure across the island makes the grid more susceptible to damage from storms; the median age of PREPA power plants is 44\xc2\xa0years. Inadequate safety also plagues the company and local newspapers frequently describe poor maintenance and outdated controls.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-64">\n        <a href="#cite_note-64">\n         [64]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The island\'s water system was also troubled before the hurricanes. Seventy percent of the island had water that didn\'t meet the standards of the 1974\n       <a href="/wiki/Safe_Drinking_Water_Act" title="Safe Drinking Water Act">\n        Safe Drinking Water Act\n       </a>\n       , according to the\n       <a href="/wiki/Natural_Resources_Defense_Council" title="Natural Resources Defense Council">\n        Natural Resources Defense Council\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-65">\n        <a href="#cite_note-65">\n         [65]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Evacuation orders were issued in Puerto Rico in advance of Maria, and officials announced that 450 shelters would open in the afternoon of September 18.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-66">\n        <a href="#cite_note-66">\n         [66]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       As of September 19, at least 2,000 people in Puerto Rico had sought shelter.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-67">\n        <a href="#cite_note-67">\n         [67]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Mainland_United_States">\n        Mainland United States\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Maria&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Mainland United States">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       As Maria approached the coast of\n       <a href="/wiki/North_Carolina" title="North Carolina">\n        North Carolina\n       </a>\n       and threatened to bring tropical storm conditions, a storm surge warning was issued for the coast between\n       <a href="/wiki/Ocracoke_Inlet" title="Ocracoke Inlet">\n        Ocracoke Inlet\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Cape_Hatteras" title="Cape Hatteras">\n        Cape Hatteras\n       </a>\n       , while a storm surge watch was issued for the\n       <a href="/wiki/Pamlico_Sound" title="Pamlico Sound">\n        Pamlico Sound\n       </a>\n       , the lower\n       <a href="/wiki/Neuse_River" title="Neuse River">\n        Neuse River\n       </a>\n       , and the\n       <a href="/wiki/Alligator_River_(North_Carolina)" title="Alligator River (North Carolina)">\n        Alligator River\n       </a>\n       on the morning of September 26. A state of emergency was declared by officials in\n       <a href="/wiki/Dare_County,_North_Carolina" title="Dare County, North Carolina">\n        Dare\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Hyde_County,_North_Carolina" title="Hyde County, North Carolina">\n        Hyde\n       </a>\n       counties, while visitors were ordered to evacuate\n       <a href="/wiki/Hatteras_Island" title="Hatteras Island">\n        Hatteras\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ocracoke_Island" title="Ocracoke Island">\n        Ocracoke\n       </a>\n       islands.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-newsobserver_68-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-newsobserver-68">\n         [68]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Ferry service between\n       <a href="/wiki/Ocracoke,_North_Carolina" title="Ocracoke, North Carolina">\n        Ocracoke\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Cedar_Island,_North_Carolina" title="Cedar Island, North Carolina">\n        Cedar Island\n       </a>\n       was suspended the evening of September 25, and remained suspended on September 26 and 27, due to rough seas, while ferry service between Ocracoke and Hatteras Island was suspended on September 26 and 27.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-newsobserver_68-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-newsobserver-68">\n         [68]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-newsobserver2_69-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-newsobserver2-69">\n         [69]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The port in\n       <a href="/wiki/Morehead_City,_North_Carolina" title="Morehead City, North Carolina">\n        Morehead City\n       </a>\n       was closed by the\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Coast_Guard" title="United States Coast Guard">\n        United States Coast Guard\n       </a>\n       on the morning of September 26.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-newsobserver_68-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-newsobserver-68">\n         [68]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Schools in Dare County closed on September 26 and 27, while schools in\n       <a href="/wiki/Carteret_County,_North_Carolina" title="Carteret County, North Carolina">\n        Carteret\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Tyrrell_County,_North_Carolina" title="Tyrrell County, North Carolina">\n        Tyrrell\n       </a>\n       counties, along with Ocracoke Island, dismissed early on September 26, in anticipation of high winds.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-newsobserver_68-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-newsobserver-68">\n         [68]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-newsobserver2_69-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-newsobserver2-69">\n         [69]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Schools in\n       <a href="/wiki/Currituck_County,_North_Carolina" title="Currituck County, North Carolina">\n        Currituck County\n       </a>\n       were closed on September 27, due to high winds.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-newsobserver2_69-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-newsobserver2-69">\n         [69]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Impact_in_the_Lesser_Antilles">\n        Impact in the Lesser Antilles\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Maria&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Impact in the Lesser Antilles">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Windward_Islands">\n        Windward Islands\n       <span class="sortkey" style="display:none">\n          7010500000000000000\xe2\x99\xa0\n         </span>\n         $50\xc2\xa0billion\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <sup      <td class="table-na" data-sort-value="" style="background: #ececec; color: #2C2C2C; vertical-align: middle; font-size: smaller; text-align: center;">\n         N/A\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-StCroixHeartAttack_82-0">\n          <a href="#cite_note-StCroixHeartAttack-82">\n           [82]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </td>\n data-sort-value="" style="background: #ececec; color: #2C2C2C; vertical-align: middle; font-size: smaller; text-align: center;">\n         N/A\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-83">\n          <a href="#cite_note-83">\n           [83]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-4th_US_death_84-0">\n          <a href="#cite_note-4th_US_death-84">\n           [84]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr class="sortbottom">\n        <th scope="row" style="text-align: lefit;">\n         Totals:\n        </th>\n        <th style="text-align:right;">\n         <span class="sortkey" style="display:none">\n          7001670000000000000\xe2\x99\xa0\n         </span>\n
