</th>\n        <th style="text-align:right;">\n         <span class="sortkey" style="display:none">\n          7001990000000000000\xe2\x99\xa0\n         </span>\n         99\n        </th>\n        <th style="text-align:right;">\n         &gt;\n         <span class="sortkey" style="display:none">\n          7010511960000000000\xe2\x99\xa0\n         </span>\n         $51.2\xc2\xa0billion\n        </th>\n        <th>\n        </th>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       The outer\n       <a href="/wiki/Rainband" title="Rainband">\n        rainbands\n       </a>\n       of Maria produced heavy rainfall and strong gusts across the southern\n       <a href="/wiki/Windward_Islands" title="Windward Islands">\n        Windward Islands\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-85">\n        <a href="#cite_note-85">\n         [85]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Hewanorra_International_Airport" title="Hewanorra International Airport">\n        Hewanorra\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/George_F._L._Charles_Airport" title="George F. L. Charles Airport">\n        George F. L. Charles\n       </a>\n       airports of\n       <a href="/wiki/Saint_Lucia" title="Saint Lucia">\n        Saint Lucia\n       </a>\n       respectively recorded 4.33\xc2\xa0in (110\xc2\xa0mm) and 3.1\xc2\xa0in (80\xc2\xa0mm) of rain, though even higher quantities fell elsewhere on the island.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-86">\n        <a href="#cite_note-86">\n         [86]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Scattered rock slides, landslides and uprooted trees caused minor damage and blocked some roads.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-stluciarock_87-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-stluciarock-87">\n         [87]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Several districts experienced localized blackouts due to downed or damaged power lines.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-88">\n        <a href="#cite_note-88">\n         [88]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The agricultural sector, especially the banana industry, suffered losses from the winds.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-stluciarock_87-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-stluciarock-87">\n         [87]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Heavy rainfall amounting to 3\xe2\x80\x935\xc2\xa0in (75\xe2\x80\x93125\xc2\xa0mm)\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-89">\n        <a href="#cite_note-89">\n         [89]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       caused scattered flooding across\n       <a href="/wiki/Barbados" title="Barbados">\n        Barbados\n       </a>\n       ; in\n       <a href="/wiki/Christ_Church,_Barbados" title="Christ Church, Barbados">\n        Christ Church\n       </a>\n       , the flood waters trapped residents from the neighborhood of\n       <a href="/wiki/Christ_Church,_Barbados#Towns.2C_villages.2C_and_hamlets" title="Christ Church, Barbados">\n        Goodland\n       </a>\n       in their homes and inundated the business streets of\n       <a href="/wiki/Saint_Lawrence_Gap" title="Saint Lawrence Gap">\n        Saint Lawrence Gap\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-90">\n        <a href="#cite_note-90">\n         [90]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-91">\n        <a href="#cite_note-91">\n         [91]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Maria stirred up rough seas that flooded coastal sidewalks in\n       <a href="/wiki/Bridgetown" title="Bridgetown">\n        Bridgetown\n       </a>\n       and damaged boats as operators had difficulties securing their vessels.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-92">\n        <a href="#cite_note-92">\n         [92]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       High winds triggered an island-wide power outage and downed a coconut tree onto a residence in\n       <a href="/wiki/Saint_Joseph,_Barbados" title="Saint Joseph, Barbados">\n        Saint Joseph\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-93">\n        <a href="#cite_note-93">\n         [93]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-94">\n        <a href="#cite_note-94">\n         [94]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Passing 30\xc2\xa0mi (50\xc2\xa0km) off the northern shorelines, Maria brought torrential rainfall and strong gusts to Martinique but spared the island of its hurricane-force windfield,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-frenchislands_95-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-frenchislands-95">\n         [95]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       which at the time extended 25\xc2\xa0mi (35\xc2\xa0km) around the eye.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-96">\n        <a href="#cite_note-96">\n         [96]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The commune of\n       <a href="/wiki/Le_Marigot" title="Le Marigot">\n        Le Marigot\n       </a>\n       recorded 6.7\xc2\xa0inches (170\xc2\xa0mm) of rain over a 24-hour period.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-rainfall_97-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-rainfall-97">\n         [97]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       By September 19, Maria had knocked out power to 70,000 households, about 40% of the population.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-lci_98-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-lci-98">\n         [98]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Water service was cut to 50,000 customers, especially in the communes of\n       <a href="/wiki/Le_Morne-Rouge" title="Le Morne-Rouge">\n        Le Morne-Rouge\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Gros-Morne,_Martinique" title="Gros-Morne, Martinique">\n        Gros-Morne\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-frenchislands_95-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-frenchislands-95">\n         [95]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-interieur_99-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-interieur-99">\n         [99]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Numerous roads and streets, especially along the northern coast, were impassible due to rock slides, fallen trees and toppled power poles.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-interieur_99-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-interieur-99">\n         [99]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-lci_98-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-lci-98">\n         [98]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Streets in\n       <a href="/wiki/Fort-de-France" title="Fort-de-France">\n        Fort-de-France\n       </a>\n       were inundated.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-frenchislands_95-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-frenchislands-95">\n         [95]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In the seaside commune of\n       <a href="/wiki/Le_Carbet" title="Le Carbet">\n        Le Carbet\n       </a>\n       , rough seas washed ashore large rocks and demolished some coastal structures,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-frenchislands_95-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-frenchislands-95">\n         [95]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nytimescarib_100-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-nytimescarib-100">\n         [100]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       while some boats were blown over along the bay of the commune of\n       <a href="/wiki/Sch%C5%93lcher" title="Sch\xc5\x93lcher">\n        Sch\xc5\x93lcher\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-101">\n        <a href="#cite_note-101">\n         [101]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Martinique\'s agricultural sector suffered considerable losses: about 70% of banana crops sustained wind damage, with nearly every tree downed along the northern coast.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-cropsfrench_102-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-cropsfrench-102">\n         [102]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       There were no deaths on the island, although four people were injured in the hurricane\xe2\x80\x94two seriously and two lightly.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-interieur_99-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-interieur-99">\n         [99]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Dominica">\n        Dominica\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Maria&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Dominica">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:292px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Aerial_view_of_part_of_Roseau,_the_capital_city_of_Dominica.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3840" data-file-width="5760" height="193" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ce/Aerial_view_of_part_of_Roseau%2C_the_capital_city_of_Dominica.jpg/290px-Aerial_view_of_part_of_Roseau%2C_the_capital_city_of_Dominica.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ce/Aerial_view_of_part_of_Roseau%2C_the_capital_city_of_Dominica.jpg/435px-Aerial_view_of_part_of_Roseau%2C_the_capital_city_of_Dominica.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ce/Aerial_view_of_part_of_Roseau%2C_the_capital_city_of_Dominica.jpg/580px-Aerial_view_of_part_of_Roseau%2C_the_capital_city_of_Dominica.jpg 2x" width="290"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Aerial_view_of_part_of_Roseau,_the_capital_city_of_Dominica.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         An aerial view of part of Roseau, revealing widespread damage to roofs. Flash floods clogged roads with debris \xe2\x80\x93 vegetative and structural \xe2\x80\x93 and mud.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Rainfall ahead of the hurricane caused several landslides in Dominica as water levels across the island began to rise by the afternoon of September 18.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-before_103-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-before-103">\n         [103]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Maria made landfall at 21:15\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Atlantic_Standard_Time" title="Atlantic Standard Time">\n        AST\n       </a>\n       that day (1:15\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UTC" title="UTC">\n        UTC\n       </a>\n       , September 19) as a Category\xc2\xa05 hurricane with\n       <a href="/wiki/Maximum_sustained_wind" title="Maximum sustained wind">\n        maximum sustained winds\n       </a>\n       of 160\xc2\xa0mph (260\xc2\xa0km/h).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Dominica_landfall_TCU_23-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Dominica_landfall_TCU-23">\n         [23]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       These winds, the most extreme to ever impact the island,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-104">\n        <a href="#cite_note-104">\n         [104]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       battered the roof of practically every home\xe2\x80\x94including the\n       <a href="/wiki/Official_residence" title="Official residence">\n        official residence\n       </a>\n       of\n       <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Dominica" title="Prime Minister of Dominica">\n        Prime Minister\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Roosevelt_Skerrit" title="Roosevelt Skerrit">\n        Roosevelt Skerrit\n       </a>\n       , who required rescue when his home began to flood.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-IBtimes_PM_roof_105-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-IBtimes_PM_roof-105">\n         [105]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Downing all cellular, radio and internet services, Maria effectively cut Dominica off from the outside world; the situation there remained unclear for a couple of days after the hurricane\'s passage.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nytimedom_106-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-nytimedom-106">\n         [106]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-107">\n        <a href="#cite_note-107">\n         [107]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Skerrit called the devastation "mind boggling" before going offline, and indicated immediate priority was to rescue survivors rather than assess damage.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nytimedom_106-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-nytimedom-106">\n         [106]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Initial\n       <a href="/wiki/Amateur_radio" title="Amateur radio">\n        ham radio\n       </a>\n       reports from the capital of\n       <a href="/wiki/Roseau" title="Roseau">\n        Roseau\n       </a>\n       on September 19 indicated "total devastation," with half the city flooded, cars stranded, and stretches of residential area "flattened".\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-108">\n        <a href="#cite_note-108">\n         [108]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The next morning, the first aerial footage of Dominica elucidated the scope of the destruction.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Dominicafootage_109-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Dominicafootage-109">\n         [109]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Maria left the mountainous country blanketed in a field of debris: Rows of houses along the entirety of the coastline were rendered uninhabitable, as widespread floods and landslides littered neighborhoods with the structural remnants.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Dominicafootage_109-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Dominicafootage-109">\n         [109]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-debrisfield_110-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-debrisfield-110">\n         [110]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The hurricane also inflicted extensive damage to roads and public buildings, such as schools, stores and churches,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-debrisfield_110-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-debrisfield-110">\n         [110]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and affected all of Dominica\'s 73,000 residents in some form or way.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-redcrossreport_111-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-redcrossreport-111">\n         [111]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The air control towers and terminal buildings of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Canefield_Airport" title="Canefield Airport">\n        Canefield\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Douglas%E2%80%93Charles_Airport" title="Douglas\xe2\x80\x93Charles Airport">\n        Douglas Charles\n       </a>\n       airports were severely damaged, although the runways remained relatively intact and open to emergency landings.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-redcrossreport_111-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-redcrossreport-111">\n         [111]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The disaster affected all of the island\'s 53 health facilities, including the badly damaged\n       <a href="/wiki/Princess_Margaret_Hospital_(Roseau)" title="Princess Margaret Hospital (Roseau)">\n        primary hospital\n       </a>\n       , compromising the safety of many patients.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Dominicafootage_109-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Dominicafootage-109">\n         [109]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-UNreport_112-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-UNreport-112">\n         [112]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_Maria_destruction_along_Roseau_road.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3336" data-file-width="5008" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f7/Hurricane_Maria_destruction_along_Roseau_road.jpg/220px-Hurricane_Maria_destruction_along_Roseau_road.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f7/Hurricane_Maria_destruction_along_Roseau_road.jpg/330px-Hurricane_Maria_destruction_along_Roseau_road.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f7/Hurricane_Maria_destruction_along_Roseau_road.jpg/440px-Hurricane_Maria_destruction_along_Roseau_road.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_Maria_destruction_along_Roseau_road.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         A road in the\n         <a href="/wiki/Roseau" title="Roseau">\n          Roseau\n         </a>\n         area is littered with structural debris, damaged vegetation and downed power poles and lines.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The infrastructure of Roseau was left in ruins; practically every power pole and line was downed, and the main road was reduced to fragments of flooded asphalt. The winds stripped the public library of its roof panels and demolished all but one wall of the Baptist church.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-113">\n        <a href="#cite_note-113">\n         [113]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       To the south of Roseau, riverside flooding and numerous landslides impacted the town of\n       <a href="/wiki/Pointe_Michel" title="Pointe Michel">\n        Pointe Michel\n       </a>\n       , destroying about 80% of its structures and causing most of the deaths in the country.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-pointemichel_114-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-pointemichel-114">\n         [114]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-115">\n        <a href="#cite_note-115">\n         [115]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Outside the capital area, the worst of the destruction was concentrated around the east coast and rural areas, where collapsed roads and bridges isolated many villages.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-redcrossreport_111-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-redcrossreport-111">\n         [111]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The port and fishing town of\n       <a href="/wiki/Marigot,_Dominica" title="Marigot, Dominica">\n        Marigot\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Saint_Andrew_Parish,_Dominica" title="Saint Andrew Parish, Dominica">\n        Saint Andrew Parish\n       </a>\n       , was 80% damaged.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-116">\n        <a href="#cite_note-116">\n         [116]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Settlements in\n       <a href="/wiki/Saint_David_Parish,_Dominica" title="Saint David Parish, Dominica">\n        Saint David Parish\n       </a>\n       , such as\n       <a href="/wiki/Castle_Bruce" title="Castle Bruce">\n        Castle Bruce\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Good_Hope,_Dominica" title="Good Hope, Dominica">\n        Good Hope\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Grand_Fond,_Dominica&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Grand Fond, Dominica (page does not exist)">\n        Grand Fond\n       </a>\n       , had been practically eradicated; many homes hung off cliffs or decoupled from their foundations. In\n       <a href="/wiki/Rosalie,_Dominica" title="Rosalie, Dominica">\n        Rosalie\n       </a>\n       , rushing waters gushed over the village\'s bridge and damaged facilities in its bay area. Throughout\n       <a href="/wiki/Saint_Patrick_Parish,_Dominica" title="Saint Patrick Parish, Dominica">\n        Saint Patrick Parish\n       </a>\n       , the extreme winds ripped through roofs and scorched the vegetation. Buildings in\n       <a href="/wiki/Grand_Bay,_Dominica" title="Grand Bay, Dominica">\n        Grand Bay\n       </a>\n       , the parish\'s main settlement, experienced total roof failure or were otherwise structurally compromised. Many houses in\n       <a href="/wiki/La_Plaine,_Dominica" title="La Plaine, Dominica">\n        La Plaine\n       </a>\n       caved in or slid into rivers, and its single bridge was broken.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-mariadominicareport_117-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-mariadominicareport-117">\n         [117]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Overall, the hurricane damaged the roofs of as much as 98% of the island\'s buildings,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-redcrossreport_111-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-redcrossreport-111">\n         [111]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       including those serving as shelters;\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Dominicafootage_109-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Dominicafootage-109">\n         [109]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       half of the houses had their frames destroyed.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-redcrossreport_111-4">\n        <a href="#cite_note-redcrossreport-111">\n         [111]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Its ferocious winds defoliated nearly all vegetation, splintering or uprooting thousands of trees and decimating the island\'s lush rainforests.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-118">\n        <a href="#cite_note-118">\n         [118]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The agricultural sector, a vital source of income for the country, was completely wiped out: 100% of banana and tuber plantations was lost, as well as vast amounts of livestock and farm equipment.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-redcrossreport_111-5">\n        <a href="#cite_note-redcrossreport-111">\n         [111]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In Maria\'s wake, Dominica\'s population suffered from an island-wide water shortage due to uprooted pipes. The\n       <a href="/wiki/Caribbean_Disaster_Emergency_Management_Agency" title="Caribbean Disaster Emergency Management Agency">\n        Caribbean Disaster Emergency Management Agency\n       </a>\n       (CDEMA) estimates that the hurricane has caused "billions of dollars" worth of damage.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-dominicadamage_119-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-dominicadamage-119">\n         [119]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       As of October 9, there are 28\xc2\xa0fatalities confirmed across the island, with another 32\xc2\xa0people reported missing.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-JO_Oct9_71-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-JO_Oct9-71">\n         [71]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Guadeloupe">\n        Guadeloupe\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Maria&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Guadeloupe">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:D%C3%A9gats_Ouragan_Maria_(nettoyage_des_routes).jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3343" data-file-width="4394" height="167" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/90/D%C3%A9gats_Ouragan_Maria_%28nettoyage_des_routes%29.jpg/220px-D%C3%A9gats_Ouragan_Maria_%28nettoyage_des_routes%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/90/D%C3%A9gats_Ouragan_Maria_%28nettoyage_des_routes%29.jpg/330px-D%C3%A9gats_Ouragan_Maria_%28nettoyage_des_routes%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/90/D%C3%A9gats_Ouragan_Maria_%28nettoyage_des_routes%29.jpg/440px-D%C3%A9gats_Ouragan_Maria_%28nettoyage_des_routes%29.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:D%C3%A9gats_Ouragan_Maria_(nettoyage_des_routes).jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Numerous trees fell across Guadeloupe, clogging roadways with debris\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Blustery conditions spread over\n       <a href="/wiki/Guadeloupe" title="Guadeloupe">\n        Guadeloupe\n       </a>\n       as Maria tracked to the south of the archipelago, which endured hours of unabating hurricane-force winds.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-120">\n        <a href="#cite_note-120">\n         [120]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The strongest winds blew along the southern coastlines of\n       <a href="/wiki/Basse-Terre_Island" title="Basse-Terre Island">\n        Basse-Terre Island\n       </a>\n       :\n       <a href="/wiki/Gourbeyre" title="Gourbeyre">\n        Gourbeyre\n       </a>\n       observed a peak wind speed of 101 mph (162\xc2\xa0km/h), while winds up north in nearby\n       <a href="/wiki/Baillif" title="Baillif">\n        Baillif\n       </a>\n       reached 92\xc2\xa0mph (148\xc2\xa0km/h).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-guadeloupemeteo_121-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-guadeloupemeteo-121">\n         [121]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Along those regions, the hurricane kicked up extremely rough seas with 20\xc2\xa0ft (6\xc2\xa0m) waves.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-waves_122-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-waves-122">\n         [122]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The combination of rough seas and winds was responsible for widespread structural damage and flooding throughout the archipelago, especially from Pointe-\xc3\xa0-Pitre, along\n       <a href="/wiki/Grande-Terre" title="Grande-Terre">\n        Grand-Terre Island\n       </a>\n       \'s southwestern coast, to\n       <a href="/wiki/Petit-Bourg" title="Petit-Bourg">\n        Petit-Bourg\n       </a>\n       and the southern coasts on Basse-Terre Island.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-MariaGuadeloupe_74-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-MariaGuadeloupe-74">\n         [74]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Aside from wind-related effects, rainfall from Maria was also significant. In just a day, the hurricane dropped nearly a month\'s worth of rainfall at some important locations:\n       <a href="/wiki/Pointe-%C3%A0-Pitre" title="Pointe-\xc3\xa0-Pitre">\n        Pointe-\xc3\xa0-Pitre\n       </a>\n       recorded a 24-hour total of 7.5\xc2\xa0inches (191\xc2\xa0mm), while the capital of\n       <a href="/wiki/Basse-Terre" title="Basse-Terre">\n        Basse-Terre\n       </a>\n       measured 6.4\xc2\xa0in (163\xc2\xa0mm).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-rainfall_97-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-rainfall-97">\n         [97]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Even greater quantities fell at higher elevations of Basse Terre Island, with a maximum total of 18.07\xc2\xa0in (459\xc2\xa0mm) measured at the mountainous locality of\n       <a href="/wiki/Matouba" title="Matouba">\n        Matouba\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Saint-Claude,_Guadeloupe" title="Saint-Claude, Guadeloupe">\n        Saint-Claude\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-guadeloupemeteo_121-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-guadeloupemeteo-121">\n         [121]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Throughout the archipelago, the hurricane left 40% of the population (80,000 households) without power and 25% of landline users without service.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-guadeloupetrees_123-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-guadeloupetrees-123">\n         [123]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The islands of\n       <a href="/wiki/Marie-Galante" title="Marie-Galante">\n        Marie-Galante\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/La_D%C3%A9sirade" title="La D\xc3\xa9sirade">\n        La D\xc3\xa9sirade\n       </a>\n       and especially\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Les_Saintes" title="Les Saintes">\n        Les Saintes\n       </a>\n       bore the brunt of the winds, which caused heavy damage to structures and nature alike and cut the islands off from their surroundings for several days.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-MariaGuadeloupe_74-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-MariaGuadeloupe-74">\n         [74]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-guadeloupetrees_123-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-guadeloupetrees-123">\n         [123]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Homes on\n       <a href="/wiki/Terre-de-Haut_Island" title="Terre-de-Haut Island">\n        Terre-de-Haut Island\n       </a>\n       of Les Saintes were flooded or lost their roofs.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-124">\n        <a href="#cite_note-124">\n         [124]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On the mainland, sections of Pointe-\xc3\xa0-Pitre stood under more than 3.3\xc2\xa0feet (1\xc2\xa0m) of water, and the city\'s hospital sustained significant damage.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-interieur_99-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-interieur-99">\n         [99]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The Basse-Terre region suffered severe damage to nearly 100% of its banana crops, comrpising a total area of more than 5,000\n       <a href="/wiki/Acre" title="Acre">\n        acres\n       </a>\n       (2,000\n       <a href="/wiki/Hectare" title="Hectare">\n        hectares\n       </a>\n       ); farmers described the destruction to their plantations as "complete annihilation".\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-cropsfrench_102-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-cropsfrench-102">\n         [102]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Beyond their impact on farmland, the strong winds ravaged much of the island\'s vegetation: fallen trees and branches covered practically every major road and were responsible for one death.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-guadeloupetrees_123-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-guadeloupetrees-123">\n         [123]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Another person was killed upon being swept out to sea.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-MariaGuadeloupe_74-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-MariaGuadeloupe-74">\n         [74]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Two people disappeared at sea after their vessel capsized offshore\n       <a href="/wiki/La_D%C3%A9sirade" title="La D\xc3\xa9sirade">\n        La D\xc3\xa9sirade\n       </a>\n       , east of mainland\n       <a href="/wiki/Grande-Terre" title="Grande-Terre">\n        Grande-Terre\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-guadeloupetrees_123-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-guadeloupetrees-123">\n         [123]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Damage from Maria across Guadeloupe amounted to at least \xe2\x82\xac100 million (US$120 million).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-dmgguadeloupe_125-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-dmgguadeloupe-125">\n         [125]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="United_States_Virgin_Islands">\n        United States Virgin Islands\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Maria&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: United States Virgin Islands">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Maria\'s outer eyewall was reported by the National Hurricane Center to have crossed\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Saint_Croix" title="Saint Croix">\n        Saint Croix\n       </a>\n       while the hurricane was at Category 5 intensity. The hurricane caused extensive and severe damage to the island. Sustained winds at the\n       <a href="/wiki/Sandy_Point_National_Wildlife_Refuge" title="Sandy Point National Wildlife Refuge">\n        Sandy Point National Wildlife Refuge\n       </a>\n       reached 99 to 104\xc2\xa0mph (159 to 167\xc2\xa0km/h) and gusted to 137\xc2\xa0mph (220\xc2\xa0km/h).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-126">\n        <a href="#cite_note-126">\n         [126]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The Luis Hospital suffered roof damage and flooding, but remained operational.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-127">\n        <a href="#cite_note-127">\n         [127]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       One person died from a storm-induced heart attack.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-StCroixHeartAttack_82-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-StCroixHeartAttack-82">\n         [82]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Impact_in_the_Greater_Antilles_and_the_United_States">\n        Impact in the Greater Antilles and the United States\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Maria&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Impact in the Greater Antilles and the United States">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Puerto_Rico_2">\n        Puerto Rico\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Maria&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Puerto Rico">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="wikitable" style="float:right; clear:right; margin:0.5em 0 0.5em 1em;">\n       <caption>\n        Wettest tropical cyclones and their remnants in Puerto Rico\n        <br/>\n        <small>\n         Highest-known totals\n        </small>\n       </caption>\n       <tr>\n        <th colspan="3" scope="col">\n         Precipitation\n        </th>\n        <th rowspan="2" scope="col">\n         Storm\n        </th>\n        <th rowspan="2" scope="col">\n         Location\n        </th>\n        <th class="unsortable" rowspan="2" scope="col">\n         <abbr title="Reference">\n          Ref.\n         </abbr>\n        </th>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="col">\n         Rank\n        </th>\n        <th scope="col">\n         <abbr title="millimetres">\n          mm\n         </abbr>\n        </th>\n        <th scope="col">\n         <abbr title="inches">\n          in\n         </abbr>\n        </th>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         1\n        </td>\n        <td style="text-align:right;">\n         1,058.7\n        </td>\n        <td style="text-align:right;">\n         41.68\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/Tropical_Depression_Fifteen_(1970)" title="Tropical Depression Fifteen (1970)">\n          T.  [129]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         3\n        </td>\n        <td style="text-align:right;">\n         845.6\n        </td>\n        <td style="text-align:right;">\n         33.29\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Eloise" title="Hurricane Eloise">\n          Eloise 1975\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         Dos Bocas\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WPCMAX_128-1">\n          <a href="#cite_note-WPCMAX-128">\n           [128]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         4\n        </td>\n        <td style="text-align:right;">\n         804.4\n        </td>\n        <td </a>\n         </sup>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         5\n        </td>\n        <td style="text-align:right;">\n         775.0\n        </td>\n        <td style="text-align:right;">\n         30.51\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Georges" title="Hurricane Georges">\n          Georges 1998\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         Jayuya\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WPCMAX_128-2">\n          <a href="#cite_note-WPCMAX-128">\n           [128]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         6\n        </td>\n        <td style="text-align:right;">\n         662.2\n        </td>\n        <td style="text-align:right;">\n         26.07\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Hazel" title="Hurricane Hazel">\n          Hazel 1954\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         Toro Negro Tunnel\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-131">\n          <a href="#cite_note-131">\n           [131]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         7\n        </td>\n        <td style="text-align:right;">\n         652.5\n        </td>\n        <td </td>\n        <td>\n         Guavate Camp\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WPCMAX_128-3">\n          <a href="#cite_note-WPCMAX-128">\n           [128]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         8\n        </td>\n        <td style="text-align:right;">\n         596.4\n        </td>\n        <td style="text-align:right;">\n         23.48\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Hortense" title="Hurricane Hortense">\n          Hortense 1996\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         Cayey 1 NW\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WPCMAX_128-4">\n          <a href="#cite_note-WPCMAX-128">\n           [128]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         9\n        </td>\n        <td style="text-align:right;">\n         584.2\n        </td>\n        <td style="text-align:right;">\n         23.00\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/1899_San_Ciriaco_hurricane" title="1899 San Ciriaco hurricane">\n          1899 San Ciriaco hurricane\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/Adjuntas,_Puerto_Rico" title="Adjuntas, Puerto Rico">\n          Adjuntas\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-132">\n          <a href="#cite_note-132">\n           [132]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         10\n        </td>\n        <td style="text-align:right;">\n         560.1\n        </td>\n        <td style="text-align:right;">\n         22.05\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Irene" title="Hurricane Irene">\n          Irene 2011\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         Gurabo Abajo\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Irene_11_133-0">\n          <a href="#cite_note-Irene_11-133">\n           [133]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       The storm made landfall on Puerto Rico on Wednesday, September 20.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NYT20170920_134-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NYT20170920-134">\n         [134]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       A sustained wind of 64\xc2\xa0mph (103\xc2\xa0km/h) with a gust to 113\xc2\xa0mph (182\xc2\xa0km/h) was reported in San Juan, Puerto Rico, immediately prior to the hurricane making landfall on the island. After landfall, wind gusts of 109\xc2\xa0mph (175\xc2\xa0km/h) were reported at Yabucoa Harbor and 118\xc2\xa0mph (190\xc2\xa0km/h) at Camp Santiago.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-135">\n        <a href="#cite_note-135">\n         [135]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In addition, very heavy rainfall occurred throughout the territory, peaking at 37.9\xc2\xa0in (962.7\xc2\xa0mm) in\n       <a href="/wiki/Caguas,_Puerto_Rico" title="Caguas, Puerto Rico">\n        Caguas\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-136">\n        <a href="#cite_note-136">\n         [136]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Widespread flooding affected San Juan, waist-deep in some areas, and numerous structures lost their roof.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NYT20170920_134-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NYT20170920-134">\n         [134]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The coastal\n       <a href="/wiki/La_Perla,_San_Juan,_Puerto_Rico" title="La Perla, San Juan, Puerto Rico">\n        La Perla neighborhood\n       </a>\n       of San Juan was largely destroyed.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-137">\n        <a href="#cite_note-137">\n         [137]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cata%C3%B1o" title="Cata\xc3\xb1o">\n        Cata\xc3\xb1o\n       </a>\n       saw extensive damage, with the Juana Matos neighborhood estimated to be 80\xc2\xa0percent destroyed.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NYT_Sep21_138-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NYT_Sep21-138">\n         [138]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The primary airport in San Juan, the\n       <a href="/wiki/Luis_Mu%C3%B1oz_Mar%C3%ADn_International_Airport" title="Luis Mu\xc3\xb1oz Mar\xc3\xadn International Airport">\n        Luis Mu\xc3\xb1oz Mar\xc3\xadn International Airport\n       </a>\n       , was slated to reopen on September 22.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-139">\n        <a href="#cite_note-139">\n         [139]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       <a href="/wiki/Storm_surge" title="Storm surge">\n        Storm surge\n       </a>\n       and flash flooding\xe2\x80\x94stemming from flood gate releases at\n       <a href="/wiki/La_Plata_Lake" title="La Plata Lake">\n        La Plata Lake\n       </a>\n       Dam\xe2\x80\x94converged on the town of\n       <a href="/wiki/Toa_Baja,_Puerto_Rico" title="Toa Baja, Puerto Rico">\n        Toa Baja\n       </a>\n       , trapping thousands of residents. Survivors indicate that flood waters rose at least 6\xc2\xa0ft (1.8\xc2\xa0m) in 30\xc2\xa0minutes, with flood waters reaching a depth of 15\xc2\xa0ft (4.6\xc2\xa0m) in some areas. More than 2,000\xc2\xa0people were rescued once military relief reached the town 24\xc2\xa0hours after the storm. At least eight people died due to the flooding while many are unaccounted for.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ToaBaja_140-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ToaBaja-140">\n         [140]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_Maria_(2017)_170923-H-NI589-0007_(36602415074).jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3744" data-file-width="5616" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/Hurricane_Maria_%282017%29_170923-H-NI589-0007_%2836602415074%29.jpg/220px-Hurricane_Maria_%282017%29_170923-H-NI589-0007_%2836602415074%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/Hurricane_Maria_%282017%29_170923-H-NI589-0007_%2836602415074%29.jpg/330px-Hurricane_Maria_%282017%29_170923-H-NI589-0007_%2836602415074%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/Hurricane_Maria_%282017%29_170923-H-NI589-0007_%2836602415074%29.jpg/440px-Hurricane_Maria_%282017%29_170923-H-NI589-0007_%2836602415074%29.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_Maria_(2017)_170923-H-NI589-0007_(36602415074).jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Thousands of homes suffered varying degrees of damage while large swaths of vegetation were shredded by the hurricane\'s violent winds\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       As of October 14, the death toll stood at 48, with about 117 people missing.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CNNOct14_141-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CNNOct14-141">\n         [141]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On September 24, Governor Rossell\xc3\xb3 estimated that the damage from Hurricane Maria in Puerto Rico was surely over the $8 billion damage by Hurricane Georges.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-tallies_up_142-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-tallies_up-142">\n         [142]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Approximately 80\xc2\xa0percent of the territory\'s agriculture was lost due to the hurricane, with agricultural losses estimated at $780\xc2\xa0million.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-143">\n        <a href="#cite_note-143">\n         [143]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The hurricane completely destroyed the island\'s power grid, leaving all 3.4\xc2\xa0million residents without electricity.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NYT_Sep21_138-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NYT_Sep21-138">\n         [138]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NBCNY_Sep22_144-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NBCNY_Sep22-144">\n         [144]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-145">\n        <a href="#cite_note-145">\n         [145]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Puerto Rican governor\n       <a href="/wiki/Ricardo_Rossell%C3%B3" title="Ricardo Rossell\xc3\xb3">\n        Ricardo Rossell\xc3\xb3\n       </a>\n       stated that it could take months to restore power in some locations,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-146">\n        <a href="#cite_note-146">\n         [146]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       with San Juan Mayor\n       <a href="/wiki/Carmen_Yul%C3%ADn_Cruz" title="Carmen Yul\xc3\xadn Cruz">\n        Carmen Yul\xc3\xadn Cruz\n       </a>\n       estimating that some areas would remain without power for four to six months.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-147">\n        <a href="#cite_note-147">\n         [147]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Communication networks were crippled across the island. Ninety-five percent of cell networks were down with 48 of the island\'s 78 counties networks being completely inoperable.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NBCNY_Sep22_144-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NBCNY_Sep22-144">\n         [144]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Eighty-five per cent of above-ground phone and internet cables were knocked out.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-148">\n        <a href="#cite_note-148">\n         [148]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Only one radio station,\n       <a href="/wiki/WAPA_(AM)" title="WAPA (AM)">\n        WAPA 680 AM\n       </a>\n       , remained on-air through the storm.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NBCNY_Sep22_144-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NBCNY_Sep22-144">\n         [144]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:142px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Puerto_Rico_weather_radar_after_Hurricane_Maria_(2).png">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1008" data-file-width="756" height="187" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/23/Puerto_Rico_weather_radar_after_Hurricane_Maria_%282%29.png/140px-Puerto_Rico_weather_radar_after_Hurricane_Maria_%282%29.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/23/Puerto_Rico_weather_radar_after_Hurricane_Maria_%282%29.png/210px-Puerto_Rico_weather_radar_after_Hurricane_Maria_%282%29.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/23/Puerto_Rico_weather_radar_after_Hurricane_Maria_%282%29.png/280px-Puerto_Rico_weather_radar_after_Hurricane_Maria_%282%29.png 2x" width="140"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Puerto_Rico_weather_radar_after_Hurricane_Maria_(2).png" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         NEXRAD radar destroyed by Maria\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/NEXRAD" title="NEXRAD">\n        NEXRAD\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Weather_radar" title="Weather radar">\n        Doppler weather radar\n       </a>\n       of Puerto Rico has also been literally blown away. The\n       <a href="/wiki/Radome" title="Radome">\n        radome\n       </a>\n       which covers the radar antenna, and which had to withstand winds of more than 130 mph, was destroyed while the antenna of 30 feet in diameter was blown from the pedestal, the latter remaining intact. The radar is 2800 feet above sea level and the anemometer at the site measured winds of about 145 mph before communications broke, which means winds at that height were likely 20 percent higher than what was seen at sea level. Its replacement will take a few months.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WTC-radar_149-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-WTC-radar-149">\n         [149]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The nearby island of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Vieques" title="Vieques">\n        Vieques\n       </a>\n       suffered similarly extensive damage. Communications were largely lost across the island. Widespread property destruction took place with many structures leveled.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-150">\n        <a href="#cite_note-150">\n         [150]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <div class="PopUpMediaTransform" id="mwe_player_2" style="width:220px;" videopayload=\'&lt;div class="mediaContainer" style="width:854px"&gt;&lt;video id="mwe_player_3" poster="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f4/Hurricane_Maria_at_Coast_Guard_Sector_San_Juan.webm/854px--Hurricane_Maria_at_Coast_Guard_Sector_San_Juan.webm.jpg" controls="" preload="none" autoplay="" style="width:854px;height:480px" class="kskin" data-durationhint="31.801" data-startoffset="0" data-mwtitle="Hurricane_Maria_at_Coast_Guard_Sector_San_Juan.webm" data-mwprovider="wikimediacommons"&gt;&lt;source src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/transcoded/f/f4/Hurricane_Maria_at_Coast_Guard_Sector_San_Juan.webm/Hurricane_Maria_at_Coast_Guard_Sector_San_Juan.webm.480p.webm" type="video/webm; codecs=&amp;quot;vp8, vorbis&amp;quot;" data-title="WebM (360P)" data-shorttitle="WebM 360P" data-transcodekey="360p.webm" data-width="640" data-height="360" data-bandwidth="575552" data-framerate="29.97"/&gt;&lt;/video&gt;&lt;/div&gt;\'>\n         <img alt="File:Hurricane Maria at Coast Guard Sector San Juan.webm" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f4/Hurricane_Maria_at_Coast_Guard_Sector_San_Juan.webm/220px--Hurricane_Maria_at_Coast_Guard_Sector_San_Juan.webm.jpg" style="width:220px;height:124px"/>\n         <a href="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/f/f4/Hurricane_Maria_at_Coast_Guard_Sector_San_Juan.webm" target="new" title="Play media">\n          <span class="play-btn-large">\n           <span class="mw-tmh-playtext">\n            Play media\n           </span>\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </div>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_Maria_at_Coast_Guard_Sector_San_Juan.webm" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Hurricane Maria at Coast Guard Sector San Juan\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The recreational ship\n       <i>\n        Ferrel\n       </i>\n       carrying a family of four issued a distress signal while battling 20\xc2\xa0ft (6.1\xc2\xa0m) seas and 115\xc2\xa0mph (185\xc2\xa0km/h) winds on September 20.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Ferrel_151-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Ferrel-151">\n         [151]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Communications with the vessel were lost near Vieques on September 20. The\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Coast_Guard" title="United States Coast Guard">\n        United States Coast Guard\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Navy" title="United States Navy">\n        United States Navy\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/British_Royal_Navy" title="British Royal Navy">\n        British Royal Navy\n       </a>\n       conducted search-and-rescue operations utilizing an\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/HC-130" title="HC-130">\n        HC-130\n       </a>\n       aircraft, a fast response cutter,\n       <a href="/wiki/USS_Kearsarge_(LHD-3)" title="USS Kearsarge (LHD-3)">\n        USS\n        <i>\n         Kearsarge\n        </i>\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/RFA_Mounts_Bay" title="RFA Mounts Bay">\n        RFA\n        <i>\n         Mounts Bay\n        </i>\n       </a>\n       and Navy helicopters.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-152">\n        <a href="#cite_note-152">\n         [152]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On September 21, the mother and her two children were rescued while the father drowned inside the capsized vessel.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Ferrel_151-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Ferrel-151">\n         [151]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Maria\'s Category 4 winds broke a 96-foot (29\xc2\xa0m) line feed antenna of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Arecibo_Observatory" title="Arecibo Observatory">\n        Arecibo Observatory\n       </a>\n       , causing it to fall 500 feet (150\xc2\xa0m) and puncturing the dish below, greatly reducing its ability to function until repairs can be made.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-153">\n        <a href="#cite_note-153">\n         [153]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-154">\n        <a href="#cite_note-154">\n         [154]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Hispaniola">\n        Hispaniola\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Maria&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Hispaniola">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Torrential rains and strong winds impacted the\n       <a href="/wiki/Dominican_Republic" title="Dominican Republic">\n        Dominican Republic\n       </a>\n       as Maria tracked northeast of the country. Assessments on September 22 indicate 110\xc2\xa0homes were destroyed, 570 were damaged, and 3,723 were affected by flooding. Approximately 60,000\xc2\xa0people lost power in northern areas of the country. Flooding and landslides rendered many roads impassable, cutting off 38\xc2\xa0communities.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EC_Sep22_155-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-EC_Sep22-155">\n         [155]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Five people, all of them males, were killed in the Dominican Republic: four of them were of\n       <a href="/wiki/Haitians_in_the_Dominican_Republic" title="Haitians in the Dominican Republic">\n        Haitian origin\n       </a>\n       , killed when they were swept away by floodwaters; the fifth person was a Dominican man who died in a landslide.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-DRfivedeaths_72-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-DRfivedeaths-72">\n         [72]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Hurricane Maria center passed 250 km from Haiti northern coast but has received a large amount of rain and suffered some flooding. Three deaths were reported: a 45-year-old man died in the commune of Limbe, in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Nord_(Haitian_department)" title="Nord (Haitian department)">\n        department of the North\n       </a>\n       , while attempting to cross a flooded river. Two other people, a woman and a man, were mortally wounded in\n       <a href="/wiki/Cornillon,_Ouest" title="Cornillon, Ouest">\n        Cornillon\n       </a>\n       , a small town 40 kilometers east of the capital\n       <a href="/wiki/Port-au-Prince" title="Port-au-Prince">\n        Port-au-Prince\n       </a>\n       , according to the authorities.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-europe1_75-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-europe1-75">\n         [75]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Mainland_United_States_2">\n        Mainland United States\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Maria&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Mainland United States">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Maria brushed the\n       <a href="/wiki/Outer_Banks" title="Outer Banks">\n        Outer Banks\n       </a>\n       of\n       <a href="/wiki/North_Carolina" title="North Carolina">\n        North Carolina\n       </a>\n       on September 26 as the center of the storm passed by offshore and brought tropical storm conditions to the area along with a storm surge, large waves, and rip currents to the coast. The storm knocked out power to 800\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Duke_Energy_Progress" title="Duke Energy Progress">\n        Duke Energy Progress\n       </a>\n       customers in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Havelock,_North_Carolina" title="Havelock, North Carolina">\n        Havelock\n       </a>\n       area, with restoration of power expected to take several hours.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-newsobserver_68-4">\n        <a href="#cite_note-newsobserver-68">\n         [68]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Dominion_North_Carolina_Power" title="Dominion North Carolina Power">\n        Dominion North Carolina Power\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Cape_Hatteras_Electric_Cooperative" title="Cape Hatteras Electric Cooperative">\n        Cape Hatteras Electric Cooperative\n       </a>\n       experienced scattered power outages. Winds of 23\xc2\xa0mph (37\xc2\xa0km/h) and gusts of 41\xc2\xa0mph (66\xc2\xa0km/h) were reported at\n       <a href="/wiki/Dare_County_Regional_Airport" title="Dare County Regional Airport">\n        Dare County Regional Airport\n       </a>\n       at\n       <a href="/wiki/Manteo,_North_Carolina" title="Manteo, North Carolina">\n        Manteo\n       </a>\n       on September 27 while winds of 40\xc2\xa0mph (64\xc2\xa0km/h) were reported in\n       <a href="/wiki/Duck,_North_Carolina" title="Duck, North Carolina">\n        Duck\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-newsobserver2_69-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-newsobserver2-69">\n         [69]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Maria caused beach erosion at the ferry terminal at the north end of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ocracoke_Island" title="Ocracoke Island">\n        Ocracoke Island\n       </a>\n       that washed out a portion of the paved lanes where vehicles wait to board the ferry. By the morning of September 26, the storm flooded\n       <a href="/wiki/North_Carolina_Highway_12" title="North Carolina Highway 12">\n        North Carolina Highway 12\n       </a>\n       along the coast.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-newsobserver_68-5">\n        <a href="#cite_note-newsobserver-68">\n         [68]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Rip currents from Maria caused three swimmers to drown and several others to be rescued at the\n       <a href="/wiki/Jersey_Shore" title="Jersey Shore">\n        Jersey Shore\n       </a>\n       on the weekend of September 23\xe2\x80\x9324.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-156">\n        <a href="#cite_note-156">\n         [156]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       A fourth drowning death occurred in\n       <a href="/wiki/Fernandina_Beach,_Florida" title="Fernandina Beach, Florida">\n        Fernandina Beach, Florida\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-4th_US_death_84-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-4th_US_death-84">\n         [84]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Aftermath">\n        Aftermath\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Maria&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Aftermath">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Dominica_2">\n        Dominica\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Maria&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Dominica">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:242px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:An_MH-60S_Sea_Hawk_helicopter_performs_humanitarian_aid_operations._(37451428945).jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2643" data-file-width="4111" height="154" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f3/An_MH-60S_Sea_Hawk_helicopter_performs_humanitarian_aid_operations._%2837451428945%29.jpg/240px-An_MH-60S_Sea_Hawk_helicopter_performs_humanitarian_aid_operations._%2837451428945%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f3/An_MH-60S_Sea_Hawk_helicopter_performs_humanitarian_aid_operations._%2837451428945%29.jpg/360px-An_MH-60S_Sea_Hawk_helicopter_performs_humanitarian_aid_operations._%2837451428945%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f3/An_MH-60S_Sea_Hawk_helicopter_performs_humanitarian_aid_operations._%2837451428945%29.jpg/480px-An_MH-60S_Sea_Hawk_helicopter_performs_humanitarian_aid_operations._%2837451428945%29.jpg 2x" width="240"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:An_MH-60S_Sea_Hawk_helicopter_performs_humanitarian_aid_operations._(37451428945).jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         A\n         <a href="/wiki/Sikorsky_SH-60_Seahawk" title="Sikorsky SH-60 Seahawk">\n          SH-60 Seahawk\n         </a>\n         flies over Dominica en route to deliver humanitarian aid. The mountainous terrain of the island poses serious challenges to relief operations in more remote areas.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       In the wake of the hurricane, more than 85% of the island\'s houses were damaged, of which more than 25% were completely destroyed, leaving more than 50,000 of the island\'s 73,000 residents displaced.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-abcnewsdominica_157-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-abcnewsdominica-157">\n         [157]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Following the destruction of thousands of homes, most supermarkets and the water supply system, many of Dominica\'s residents were in dire need of food, water and shelter for days.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-debrisfield_110-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-debrisfield-110">\n         [110]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       With no access to electricity or running water, and with sewage systems destroyed, fears of widespread diarrhea and\n       <a href="/wiki/Dysentery" title="Dysentery">\n        dysentery\n       </a>\n       arose. The island\'s agriculture, a vital source of income for many, was obliterated as most trees were flattened. Meanwhile, the driving force of the economy\xe2\x80\x94tourism\xe2\x80\x94was expected to be scarce in the months that followed Maria. Prime Minister Roosevelt Skerrit characterized the devastation wrought by Irma and Maria as a sign of climate change and the threat it poses to the survival of his country, stating, "To deny climate change ... is to deny a truth we have just lived."\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-abcnewsdominica_157-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-abcnewsdominica-157">\n         [157]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Many islanders suffered respiratory problems as a result of excessive dust borne out of debris. Light rainfall in the weeks following Maria alleviated this problem, though it also slowed recovery efforts, particularly rebuilding damaged rooftops.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-telesur_158-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-telesur-158">\n         [158]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <table class="rquote floatright" role="presentation" style="border-collapse:collapse; border-style:none; float:right; margin:0.5em 0.75em; width:33%;">\n       <tr style="text-align:left; vertical-align:top;">\n        <td style="color:#b2b7f2; font-size:3.3em; font-family:\'Times New Roman\',serif; font-weight:bold; padding:4px 2px 2px; width:0.5em; line-height: 1em;">\n         \xe2\x80\x9c\n        </td>\n        <td style="padding:0 10px;">\n         People are trying to be strong in Dominica, like everything is fine, but its not. Everywhere needs rebuilding but there is no money to rebuild things with. OK, so we have some food and water \xe2\x80\x93 but how long for? Everything else is gone.\n        </td>\n        <td style="color:#b2b7f2; font-size:3.3em; font-family:\'Times New Roman\',serif; font-weight:bold; padding:4px 2px 2px; text-align:right; vertical-align:bottom; width:0.5em; line-height: 1em;">\n         \xe2\x80\x9d\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td class="rquotecite" colspan="3" style="padding-top:10px; font-size:smaller; line-height:1em; text-align:right;">\n         <cite>\n          \xe2\x80\x94\xc2\xa0A Dominican resident describing the state of the country five weeks after the hurricane.\n          <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-dominicaaftermath1nov_159-0">\n           <a href="#cite_note-dominicaaftermath1nov-159">\n            [159]\n           </a>\n          </sup>\n         </cite>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       Through the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Caribbean_Catastrophe_Risk_Insurance_Facility" title="Caribbean Catastrophe Risk Insurance Facility">\n        Caribbean Catastrophe Risk Insurance Facility\n       </a>\n       , Dominica received approximately US$19.2\xc2\xa0million in emergency funds.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-160">\n        <a href="#cite_note-160">\n         [160]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/USS_Wasp_(LHD-1)" title="USS Wasp (LHD-1)">\n        USS\n        <i>\n         Wasp\n        </i>\n       </a>\n       , previously deployed to\n       <a href="/wiki/Saint_Martin" title="Saint Martin">\n        Saint Martin\n       </a>\n       to assist in relief efforts after Hurricane Irma, arrived in Dominica on September 22. The vessel carried two\n       <a href="/wiki/Sikorsky_SH-60_Seahawk" title="Sikorsky SH-60 Seahawk">\n        Sikorsky SH-60 Seahawk\n       </a>\n       helicopters to assist in distribution of relief supplies in hard-to-reach areas.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-161">\n        <a href="#cite_note-161">\n         [161]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       At the\n       <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_General_Assembly" title="United Nations General Assembly">\n        United Nations General Assembly\n       </a>\n       on September 23, Prime Minister\n       <a href="/wiki/Roosevelt_Skerrit" title="Roosevelt Skerrit">\n        Roosevelt Skerrit\n       </a>\n       called the situation in Dominica an "international humanitarian emergency".\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-162">\n        <a href="#cite_note-162">\n         [162]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Royal_Canadian_Navy" title="Royal Canadian Navy">\n        Royal Canadian Navy\n       </a>\n       vessel\n       <a href="/wiki/HMCS_St._John%27s" title="HMCS St. John\'s">\n        HMCS\n        <i>\n         St. John\'s\n        </i>\n       </a>\n       was dispatched to Dominica\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-163">\n        <a href="#cite_note-163">\n         [163]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       at the request of Dominican Prime Minister Skerrit.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-164">\n        <a href="#cite_note-164">\n         [164]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The prime minister urged churches to encourage their membership to provide housing for senior citizens and disabled, many of whom remained in damaged structures despite tarpaulin donations from Venezuela, Palestine, Cuba, Jamaica, and other countries. As schools began to reopen on October\xc2\xa016, the United Nations Children\'s Fund reported that the entire child population of Dominica\xe2\x80\x9423,000 children\xe2\x80\x94remained vulnerable due to restricted access to clean drinking water.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-telesur_158-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-telesur-158">\n         [158]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Puerto_Rico_3">\n        Puerto Rico\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Maria&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Puerto Rico">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <div class="PopUpMediaTransform" id="mwe_player_4" style="width:220px;" videopayload=\'&lt;div class="mediaContainer" style="width:854px"&gt;&lt;video id="mwe_player_5" poster="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a9/US_Officials_Say_Damaged_Infrastructure_Slows_Aid_Distribution_in_Puerto_Rico.webmhd.webm/854px--US_Officials_Say_Damaged_Infrastructure_Slows_Aid_Distribution_in_Puerto_Rico.webmhd.webm.jpg" controls="" preload="none" autoplay="" style="width:854px;height:480px" class="kskin" data-durationhint="125.426" data-startoffset="0" data-mwtitle="US_Officials_Say_Damaged_Infrastructure_Slows_Aid_Distribution_in_Puerto_Rico.webmhd.webm" data-mwprovider="wikimediacommons"&gt;&lt;source src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/transcoded/a/a9/US_Officials_Say_Damaged_Infrastructure_Slows_Aid_Distribution_in_Puerto_Rico.webmhd.webm/US_Officials_Say_Damaged_Infrastructure_Slows_Aid_Distribution_in_Puerto_Rico.webmhd.webm.480p.webm" type="video/webm;
