border-style:none; float:right; margin:0.5em 0.75em; width:33%;">\n       <tr style="text-align:left; vertical-align:top;">\n        <td style="color:#b2b7f2; font-size:3.3em; font-family:\'Times New Roman\',serif; font-weight:bold; padding:4px 2px 2px; width:0.5em; line-height: 1em;">\n         \xe2\x80\x9c\n        </td>\n        <td style="padding:0 10px;">\n         There\'s a humanitarian emergency here in Puerto Rico.... This is an event without precedent.\n        </td>\n        <td style="color:#b2b7f2; font-size:3.3em; font-family:\'Times New Roman\',serif; font-weight:bold; padding:4px 2px 2px; text-align:right; vertical-align:bottom; width:0.5em; line-height: 1em;">\n         \xe2\x80\x9d\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td class="rquotecite" colspan="3" style="padding-top:10px; font-size:smaller; line-height:1em; text-align:right;">\n         <cite>\n          \xe2\x80\x94\n          <a href="/wiki/Ricardo_Rossell%C3%B3" title="Ricardo Rossell\xc3\xb3">\n           Ricardo Rossell\xc3\xb3\n          </a>\n          , Governor of Puerto Rico\n          <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ABC_Sep22_165-0">\n           <a href="#cite_note-ABC_Sep22-165">\n            [165]\n           </a>\n          </sup>\n         </cite>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       The power grid was effectively destroyed by the hurricane, leaving millions without electricity.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Power_grid_destroyed._166-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Power_grid_destroyed.-166">\n         [166]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Governor Ricardo Rossell\xc3\xb3 estimated that Maria caused at least\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/US$" title="US$">\n        US$\n       </a>\n       90 billion in damage.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-34_deaths_in_Puerto_Rico_-_90bn_in_damage_167-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-34_deaths_in_Puerto_Rico_-_90bn_in_damage-167">\n         [167]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-90_billion_168-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-90_billion-168">\n         [168]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       As of September 26, 95% of the island was without power, less than half the population had tap water, and 95% of the island had no cell phone service.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-169">\n        <a href="#cite_note-169">\n         [169]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On October 6, a little more than two weeks after the hurricane, 89% still had no power, 44% had no water service, and 58% had no cell service.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-170">\n        <a href="#cite_note-170">\n         [170]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       One month after the hurricane, 88% of the island was without power (about 3 million people), 29% lacked tap water (about 1 million people), and 40% of the island had no cell service. All hospitals were open, but most were on backup generators that provide limited power. About half of sewage treatment plants on the island were not still not functioning. FEMA reported 60,000 homes needed roofing help, and had distributed 38,000 roofing tarps.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-171">\n        <a href="#cite_note-171">\n         [171]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The island\'s highways and bridges remained heavily damaged nearly a month later. Only 392 miles of Puerto Rico\xe2\x80\x99s 5,073 miles of road were open. Some towns continue to be isolated and delivery of relief supplies including food and water are hampered-- helicopters are the only alternative.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-172">\n        <a href="#cite_note-172">\n         [172]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       As of October 1, there were ongoing fuel shortage and distribution problems, with 720 of 1,100 gas stations open.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-173">\n        <a href="#cite_note-173">\n         [173]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Guajataca_Lake" title="Guajataca Lake">\n        Guajataca Dam\n       </a>\n       was structurally damaged, and on September 22, the National Weather Service issued a\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Flash_flood_emergency" title="Flash flood emergency">\n        flash flood emergency\n       </a>\n       for parts of the area in response.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-174">\n        <a href="#cite_note-174">\n         [174]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Tens of thousands of people were ordered to evacuate the area, with about 70,000 thought to be at risk.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-175">\n        <a href="#cite_note-175">\n         [175]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The entirety of Puerto Rico was declared a Federal Disaster Zone shortly after the hurricane.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ABC_Sep22_165-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ABC_Sep22-165">\n         [165]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Federal_Emergency_Management_Agency" title="Federal Emergency Management Agency">\n        Federal Emergency Management Agency\n       </a>\n       planned to open an air bridge with three to four aircraft carrying essential supplies to the island daily starting on September 22.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NBCNY_Sep22_144-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NBCNY_Sep22-144">\n         [144]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Beyond flights involving the relief effort, limited commercial traffic resumed at\n       <a href="/wiki/Luis_Mu%C3%B1oz_Mar%C3%ADn_International_Airport" title="Luis Mu\xc3\xb1oz Mar\xc3\xadn International Airport">\n        Luis Mu\xc3\xb1oz Mar\xc3\xadn International Airport\n       </a>\n       on September 22 under primitive conditions. A dozen commercial flights operated daily as of September 26.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-176">\n        <a href="#cite_note-176">\n         [176]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       By October 3, there were 39 commercial flights per day from all Puerto Rican airports, about a quarter of the normal number.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-177">\n        <a href="#cite_note-177">\n         [177]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The next day, airports were reported to be operating at normal capacity.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-178">\n        <a href="#cite_note-178">\n         [178]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In marked contrast to the initial relief efforts for\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Katrina" title="Hurricane Katrina">\n        Hurricane Katrina\n       </a>\n       and the\n       <a href="/wiki/2010_Haiti_earthquake" title="2010 Haiti earthquake">\n        2010 Haiti earthquake\n       </a>\n       , on September 22, the only signs of relief efforts were beleaguered Puerto Rican government employees.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-On_the_Ground.2C_A_Stunned_Start_179-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-On_the_Ground.2C_A_Stunned_Start-179">\n         [179]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The territory\'s government contracted 56\xc2\xa0small companies to assist in restoring power.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ABC_Sep22_165-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ABC_Sep22-165">\n         [165]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Eight FEMA Urban Search &amp; Rescue (US&amp;R) teams were deployed to assist in rescue efforts.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FemaNewsSep25_180-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-FemaNewsSep25-180">\n         [180]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:171012-F-FH950-0642_(37634528256).jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1997" data-file-width="3000" height="146" //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/db/171012-F-FH950-0642_%2837634528256%29.jpg/440px-171012-F-FH950-0642_%2837634528256%29.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:171012-F-FH950-0642_(37634528256).jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Debris-clogged roads added to logistical challenges faced by rescue and relief crews\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       On September 24, the\n       <a href="/wiki/Amphibious_assault_ship" title="Amphibious assault ship">\n        amphibious assault ship\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/USS_Kearsarge_(LHD-3)" title="USS Kearsarge (LHD-3)">\n        USS\n        <i>\n         Kearsarge\n        </i>\n       </a>\n       and the\n       <a href="/wiki/Dock_landing_ship" title="Dock landing ship">\n        dock landing ship\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/USS_Oak_Hill_(LSD-51)" title="USS Oak Hill (LSD-51)">\n        USS\n        <i>\n         Oak Hill\n        </i>\n       </a>\n       under Rear Admiral\n       <a href="/wiki/Jeffrey_W._Hughes" title="Jeffrey W. Hughes">\n        Jeffrey W. Hughes\n       </a>\n       along with the 2,400 marines of\n       <a href="/wiki/26th_Marine_Expeditionary_Unit" title="26th Marine Expeditionary Unit">\n        26th Marine Expeditionary Unit\n       </a>\n       arrived to assist in relief efforts.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WPMoreHelp_181-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-WPMoreHelp-181">\n         [181]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-S.26S_182-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-S.26S-182">\n         [182]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-183">\n        <a href="#cite_note-183">\n         [183]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-184">\n        <a href="#cite_note-184">\n         [184]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       By September 24, there were 13 United States Coast Guard ships deployed around Puerto Rico assisting in the relief and restoration efforts: the\n       <a href="/wiki/National_Security_Cutter" title="National Security Cutter">\n        National Security Cutter\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/USCGC_James_(WMSL-754)" title="USCGC James (WMSL-754)">\n        USCGC\n        <i>\n         James\n        </i>\n       </a>\n       ; the\n       <a href="/wiki/Medium_endurance_cutter" title="Medium endurance cutter">\n        medium endurance cutters\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/USCGC_Diligence_(WMEC-616)" title="USCGC Diligence (WMEC-616)">\n        USCGC\n        <i>\n         Diligence\n        </i>\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/USCGC_Forward_(WMEC-911)" title="USCGC Forward (WMEC-911)">\n        USCGC\n        <i>\n         Forward\n        </i>\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/USCGC_Venturous_(WMEC-625)" title="USCGC Venturous (WMEC-625)">\n        USCGC\n        <i>\n         Venturous\n        </i>\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/USCGC_Valiant_(WMEC-621)" title="USCGC Valiant (WMEC-621)">\n        USCGC\n        <i>\n         Valiant\n        </i>\n       </a>\n       ; the\n       <a href="/wiki/Sentinel-class_cutter" title="Sentinel-class cutter">\n        fast response cutters\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/USCGC_Donald_Horsley" title="USCGC Donald Horsley">\n        USCGC\n        <i>\n         Donald Horsley\n        </i>\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/USCGC_Heriberto_Hernandez_(WPC-1114)" title="USCGC Heriberto Hernandez (WPC-1114)">\n        USCGC\n        <i>\n         Heriberto Hernandez\n        </i>\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/USCGC_Joseph_Napier_(WPC-1115)" title="USCGC Joseph Napier (WPC-1115)">\n        USCGC\n        <i>\n         Joseph Napier\n        </i>\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/USCGC_Richard_Dixon_(WPC-1113)" title="USCGC Richard Dixon (WPC-1113)">\n        USCGC\n        <i>\n         Richard Dixon\n        </i>\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/USCGC_Winslow_W._Griesser" title="USCGC Winslow W. Griesser">\n        USCGC\n        <i>\n         Winslow Griesser\n        </i>\n       </a>\n       ; the coastal patrol boat USCGC\n       <i>\n        Yellowfin\n       </i>\n       ; and the seagoing buoy tenders\n       <a href="/wiki/USCGC_Cypress_(WLB-210)" title="USCGC Cypress (WLB-210)">\n        USCGC\n        <i>\n         Cypress\n        </i>\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/USCGC_Elm_(WLB-204)" title="USCGC Elm (WLB-204)">\n        USCGC\n        <i>\n         Elm\n        </i>\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-185">\n        <a href="#cite_note-185">\n         [185]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Federal aid arrived on September 25 with the reopening of major ports. Eleven cargo vessels collectively carrying 1.3\xc2\xa0million liters of water, 23,000\xc2\xa0cots, and dozens of generators arrived.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-186">\n        <a href="#cite_note-186">\n         [186]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Full operations at the ports of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Guayanilla" title="Guayanilla">\n        Guayanilla\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Salinas,_Puerto_Rico" title="Salinas, Puerto Rico">\n        Salinas\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Tallaboa" title="Tallaboa">\n        Tallaboa\n       </a>\n       resumed on September 25, while the ports of San Juan,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Fajardo" title="Fajardo">\n        Fajardo\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Culebra,_Puerto_Rico" title="Culebra, Puerto Rico">\n        Culebra\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Guayama" title="Guayama">\n        Guayama\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Vieques" title="Vieques">\n        Vieques\n       </a>\n       had limited operations.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FemaNewsSep25_180-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-FemaNewsSep25-180">\n         [180]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Air_Force" title="United States Air Force">\n        United States Air Force\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Air_Mobility_Command" title="Air Mobility Command">\n        Air Mobility Command\n       </a>\n       has dedicated eight\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/C-17_Globemaster" title="C-17 Globemaster">\n        C-17 Globemaster\n       </a>\n       aircraft to deliver relief supplies.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FemaNewsSep25_180-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-FemaNewsSep25-180">\n         [180]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The Air Force assisted the\n       <a href="/wiki/Federal_Aviation_Administration" title="Federal Aviation Administration">\n        Federal Aviation Administration\n       </a>\n       with air traffic control repairs to increase throughput capacity.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FemaNewsSep25_180-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-FemaNewsSep25-180">\n         [180]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Transportation_Command" title="United States Transportation Command">\n        United States Transportation Command\n       </a>\n       has moved additional personnel and eight\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/U.S._Army" title="U.S. Army">\n        U.S. Army\n       </a>\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UH-60_Black_Hawk" title="UH-60 Black Hawk">\n        UH-60 Black Hawk\n       </a>\n       helicopters from\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Fort_Campbell,_Kentucky" title="Fort Campbell, Kentucky">\n        Fort Campbell, Kentucky\n       </a>\n       to Luis Mu\xc3\xb1oz Mar\xc3\xadn International Airport to increase distribution capacity.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FemaNewsSep25_180-4">\n        <a href="#cite_note-FemaNewsSep25-180">\n         [180]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Army_Corps_of_Engineers" title="United States Army Corps of Engineers">\n        United States Army Corps of Engineers\n       </a>\n       deployed 670 personnel engaged in assessing and restoring the power grid; as of September 25, 83 generators were installed and an additional 186 generators were en route.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FemaNewsSep25_180-5">\n        <a href="#cite_note-FemaNewsSep25-180">\n         [180]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       As of September 26, agencies of the U.S. government have delivered 4 million meals, 6 million liters of water, 70,000 tarps and 15,000 rolls of roof sheeting.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-MilTImeHospital_187-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-MilTImeHospital-187">\n         [187]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/National_Guard_of_the_United_States" title="National Guard of the United States">\n        National Guard\n       </a>\n       troops have been activated and deployed to Puerto Rico from\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Connecticut_National_Guard" title="Connecticut National Guard">\n        Connecticut\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Georgia_National_Guard" title="Georgia National Guard">\n        Georgia\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Iowa_National_Guard" title="Iowa National Guard">\n        Iowa\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Illinois_National_Guard" title="Illinois National Guard">\n        Illinois\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Kentucky_National_Guard" title="Kentucky National Guard">\n        Kentucky\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Missouri_National_Guard" title="Missouri National Guard">\n        Missouri\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/New_York_National_Guard" title="New York National Guard">\n        New York\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Rhode_Island_National_Guard" title="Rhode Island National Guard">\n        Rhode Island\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Wisconsin_National_Guard" title="Wisconsin National Guard">\n        Wisconsin\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-188">\n        <a href="#cite_note-188">\n         [188]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:20171007-_SC_National_Guard_in_Puerto_Rico_(36846539124).jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1200" data-file-width="1600" height="165" clean up efforts in\n         <a href="/wiki/Caguas,_Puerto_Rico" title="Caguas, Puerto Rico">\n          Caguas\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       On September 26, the\n       <a href="/wiki/Hospital_ship" title="Hospital ship">\n        hospital ship\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/USNS_Comfort_(T-AH-20)" title="USNS Comfort (T-AH-20)">\n        USNS\n        <i>\n         Comfort\n        </i>\n       </a>\n       prepared to deploy and subsequently arrived a week later in Puerto Rico.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-MilTImeHospital_187-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-MilTImeHospital-187">\n         [187]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-189">\n        <a href="#cite_note-189">\n         [189]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-:0_190-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-:0-190">\n         [190]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       However, most of the 250 bed floating state-of-the-art hospital has gone unused despite overburdened island clinics and hospitals. Puerto Rico\'s Department of Health is supposed to refer patients there, but there had been few referrals by October 17. Governor Rossell\xc3\xb3 explained that "The disconnect or the apparent disconnect was in the communications flow" and added "I asked for a complete revision of that so that we can now start sending more patients over there."\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-:0_190-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-:0-190">\n         [190]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       On September 27, the Pentagon reopened two major airfields on Puerto Rico and started sending aircraft, specialized units, and a hospital ship to assist in the relief effort; Brigadier General\n       <a href="/wiki/Richard_C._Kim" title="Richard C. Kim">\n        Richard C. Kim\n       </a>\n       , the deputy commanding general of\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Army_North" title="United States Army North">\n        United States Army North\n       </a>\n       , will be responsible for coordinating operations between the military, FEMA and other government agencies, and the private sector.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-191">\n        <a href="#cite_note-191">\n         [191]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Massive amounts of water, food, and fuel have either been delivered to ports in Puerto Rico or are held up at ports in the mainland United States because there is a lack of trucker drivers to move the goods into the interior; the lack of communication networks has hindered the effort as only 20% of drivers have reported to work.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-192">\n        <a href="#cite_note-192">\n         [192]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       As of September 28, the Port of San Juan has only been able to dispatch 4% of deliveries received and has very little room to accept additional shipments.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-193">\n        <a href="#cite_note-193">\n         [193]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       As of September 28, 44 percent of the population remains without drinking water and the U.S. military is shifting from "a short term, sea-based response to a predominantly land-based effort designed to provide robust, longer term support" with fuel delivery a top priority.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Army194489_194-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Army194489-194">\n         [194]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       A joint Army National Guard and Marine expeditionary unit (MEU) team has established an Installation Staging Base at the former\n       <a href="/wiki/Roosevelt_Roads_Naval_Station" title="Roosevelt Roads Naval Station">\n        Roosevelt Roads Naval Station\n       </a>\n       ; they are transporting via helicopter Department of Health and Human Services assessment teams to hospitals across Puerto Rico to determine medical requirements.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Army194489_194-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Army194489-194">\n         [194]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On September 29, the\n       <a href="/wiki/Amphibious_assault_ship" title="Amphibious assault ship">\n        amphibious assault ship\n       </a>\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/USS_Wasp_(LHD-1)" title="USS Wasp (LHD-1)">\n         USS Wasp\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       which had been providing relief activities to the island of\n       <a href="/wiki/Dominica" title="Dominica">\n        Dominica\n       </a>\n       was diverted to Puerto Rico.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-195">\n        <a href="#cite_note-195">\n         [195]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       As of September 30, FEMA official Alejandro de la Campa stated that 5% of electricity, 33% of the telecommunications infrastructure, and 50% of water services have been restored to the island.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-196">\n        <a href="#cite_note-196">\n         [196]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Residents_of_Ponce,_Puerto_Rico,_line_up_at_an_ATM_in_hopes_of_getting_some_cash._More_than_a_week_after_Hurricane_Maria_struck,_residents_are_waiting_in_long_lines_to_withdraw_money_and_for_gasoline.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="575" data-file-width="1023" height="124" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/71/Residents_of_Ponce%2C_Puerto_Rico%2C_line_up_at_an_ATM_in_hopes_of_getting_some_cash._More_than_a_week_after_Hurricane_Maria_struck%2C_residents_are_waiting_in_long_lines_to_withdraw_money_and_for_gasoline.jpg/330px-thumbnail.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/71/Residents_of_Ponce%2C_Puerto_Rico%2C_line_up_at_an_ATM_in_hopes_of_getting_some_cash._More_than_a_week_after_Hurricane_Maria_struck%2C_residents_are_waiting_in_long_lines_to_withdraw_money_and_for_gasoline.jpg/440px-thumbnail.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         More than a week after Hurricane Maria struck, residents of\n         <a href="/wiki/Ponce,_Puerto_Rico" title="Ponce, Puerto Rico">\n          Ponce, Puerto Rico\n         </a>\n         wait in long lines at an ATM to withdraw cash.\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-auto2_197-0">\n          <a href="#cite_note-auto2-197">\n           [197]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       On September 28, 2017, Lieutenant General\n       <a href="/wiki/Jeffrey_S._Buchanan" title="Jeffrey S. Buchanan">\n        Jeffrey S. Buchanan\n       </a>\n       was dispatched to\n       <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico" title="Puerto Rico">\n        Puerto Rico\n       </a>\n       to lead all military hurricane relief efforts there and to see how the military can be more effective in the recovery effort, particularly in dealing with the thousands of containers of supplies that are stuck in port because of "red tape, lack of drivers, and a crippling power outage".\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-198">\n        <a href="#cite_note-198">\n         [198]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-199">\n        <a href="#cite_note-199">\n         [199]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On September 29 he stated that there were not enough troops and equipment in place but more would be arriving soon.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-200">\n        <a href="#cite_note-200">\n         [200]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       With centralized fossil-fuel-based power plants and grid infrastructure expected to be out of commission for weeks to months, some renewable energy projects are in the works, including the shipment of hundreds of\n       <a href="/wiki/Tesla,_Inc." title="Tesla, Inc.">\n        Tesla\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Tesla_Powerwall" title="Tesla Powerwall">\n        Powerwall\n       </a>\n       battery systems to be integrated with solar PV systems\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-201">\n        <a href="#cite_note-201">\n         [201]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and Sonnen solar microgrid projects at 15 emergency community centers, the first expected to be completed in October.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-202">\n        <a href="#cite_note-202">\n         [202]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In addition, other solar companies jumped into help, including Sunnova and New Start Solar. A charity called Light Up Puerto Rico raised money to both purchase and deliver solar products, including solar panels, on Oct. 19.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-203">\n        <a href="#cite_note-203">\n         [203]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Many TV and movie stars are donating money to hurricane relief organizations to help the victims of Harvey and Maria. Prominently,\n       <a href="/wiki/Jennifer_Aniston" title="Jennifer Aniston">\n        Jennifer Aniston\n       </a>\n       has pledged a million U.S. dollars, dividing the amount equally between the\n       <a href="/wiki/International_Red_Cross_and_Red_Crescent_Movement" title="International Red Cross and Red Crescent Movement">\n        Red Cross\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=The_Ricky_Martin_Foundation_for_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="The Ricky Martin Foundation for Puerto Rico (page does not exist)">\n        The Ricky Martin Foundation for Puerto Rico\n       </a>\n       . Martin\'s foundation had raised over three million dollars as of October 13.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-204">\n        <a href="#cite_note-204">\n         [204]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       On October 10, 2017,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Carnival_Cruise_Lines" title="Carnival Cruise Lines">\n        Carnival Cruise Lines\n       </a>\n       announced that it would resume departures of cruises from San Juan on October 15, 2017.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-205">\n        <a href="#cite_note-205">\n         [205]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On October 13, both\n       <a href="/wiki/CNN" title="CNN">\n        CNN\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/The_Guardian" title="The Guardian">\n        The Guardian\n       </a>\n       reported that Puerto Ricans are drinking water being pumped from a well at an\n       <a href="/wiki/Superfund" title="Superfund">\n        EPA Superfund\n       </a>\n       site;\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-206">\n        <a href="#cite_note-206">\n         [206]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Guardian-hints_207-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Guardian-hints-207">\n         [207]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       the water was later determined to be safe to drink.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-208">\n        <a href="#cite_note-208">\n         [208]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       On October 13, the Trump administration requested $4.9 billion to fund a loan program that Puerto Rico can use to address basic functions and infrastructure needs.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-209">\n        <a href="#cite_note-209">\n         [209]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       As of October 20, only 18.5% of the island had electricity, 49.1% of cell towers were working, and 69.5% of customers had running water, with the slowest restoration in the north.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1monthstatus_210-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-1monthstatus-210">\n         [210]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Ports and commercial flights were back to normal operations, but 7.6% of USPS locations, 11.5% of supermarkets, and 21.4% of gas stations were still closed.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1monthstatus_210-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-1monthstatus-210">\n         [210]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       4,246 people were still living in emergency shelters, and tourism was down by half.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1monthstatus_210-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-1monthstatus-210">\n         [210]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       As of November 5, more than 100,000 people have left Puerto Rico for the mainland.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-211">\n        <a href="#cite_note-211">\n         [211]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Possible_leptospirosis_outbreak">\n        Possible leptospirosis outbreak\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Maria&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Possible leptospirosis outbreak">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Standing_water_in_Ponce,_Puerto_Rico,_poses_health_risks_for_its_residents_more_than_a_week_after_Hurricane_Maria_devastated_the_island.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="366" data-file-width="650" height="124" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7e/Standing_water_in_Ponce%2C_Puerto_Rico%2C_poses_health_risks_for_its_residents_more_than_a_week_after_Hurricane_Maria_devastated_the_island.jpg/220px-Standing_water_in_Ponce%2C_Puerto_Rico%2C_poses_health_risks_for_its_residents_more_than_a_week_after_Hurricane_Maria_devastated_the_island.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7e/Standing_water_in_Ponce%2C_Puerto_Rico%2C_poses_health_risks_for_its_residents_more_than_a_week_after_Hurricane_Maria_devastated_the_island.jpg/330px-Standing_water_in_Ponce%2C_Puerto_Rico%2C_poses_health_risks_for_its_residents_more_than_a_week_after_Hurricane_Maria_devastated_the_island.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7e/Standing_water_in_Ponce%2C_Puerto_Rico%2C_poses_health_risks_for_its_residents_more_than_a_week_after_Hurricane_Maria_devastated_the_island.jpg/440px-Standing_water_in_Ponce%2C_Puerto_Rico%2C_poses_health_risks_for_its_residents_more_than_a_week_after_Hurricane_Maria_devastated_the_island.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Standing_water_in_Ponce,_Puerto_Rico,_poses_health_risks_for_its_residents_more_than_a_week_after_Hurricane_Maria_devastated_the_island.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Standing water in\n         <a href="/wiki/Ponce,_Puerto_Rico" title="Ponce, Puerto Rico">\n          Ponce, Puerto Rico\n         </a>\n         more than a week after Hurricane Maria hit the island\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-auto2_197-1">\n          <a href="#cite_note-auto2-197">\n           [197]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       A possible outbreak of\n       <a href="/wiki/Leptospirosis" title="Leptospirosis">\n        leptospirosis\n       </a>\n       affected survivors in the weeks following the hurricane. The bacterial infection spreads through unsanitary water, often with contaminated animal urine. With large areas of Puerto Rico lacking clean water, residents were forced to used contaminated sources of water. As of October\xc2\xa023, at least 4\xc2\xa0people may have died from the disease while 74\xc2\xa0others are suspected of being infected. Despite the possibility of an outbreak, officials have not deemed the situation as such.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-212">\n        <a href="#cite_note-212">\n         [212]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On October 24, 2017, the number of deaths in Puerto Rico blamed on Hurricane Maria has increased to 51 with officials saying two more people died from leptospirosis in contaminated water.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-213">\n        <a href="#cite_note-213">\n         [213]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Additional_fatalities">\n        Additional fatalities\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Maria&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Additional fatalities">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <p>\n       On October 5, NPR\xc2\xa0reported an additional 49 bodies with unidentified cause of death sent to a hospital morgue since the storm.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-214">\n        <a href="#cite_note-214">\n         [214]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The\n       <i>\n        Los Angeles Times\n       </i>\n       reported 50 more deaths than normal in one region in the three days after the hurricane.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-215">\n        <a href="#cite_note-215">\n         [215]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Puerto Rico\'s\xc2\xa0Center for Investigative Reporting\xc2\xa0reported 69 hospital morgues are at \xe2\x80\x9ccapacity.\xe2\x80\x9d Exact figure is unknown.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-216">\n        <a href="#cite_note-216">\n         [216]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       According to\n       <i>\n        El Vocero\n       </i>\n       newspaper, 350 bodies are being stored at the Institute of Forensic Sciences (equivalent to the state medical examiner\'s office), many of which are still awaiting autopsies. In the report, H\xc3\xa9ctor Pesquera, secretary of the Puerto Rico Department of Public Safety, did not say how many, if any, of the cadavers were there before the storm. (On Sunday, Pesquera denied claims that there was a backlog of unexamined bodies.)\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-217">\n        <a href="#cite_note-217">\n         [217]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       On October 11,\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/Vox_(website)" title="Vox (website)">\n         Vox\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       reported 81\xc2\xa0deaths directly or indirectly related to the hurricane with another 450\xc2\xa0deaths awaiting investigation. Furthermore, they indicated 69\xc2\xa0people to be missing.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-VoxOct11_218-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-VoxOct11-218">\n         [218]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On October 14,\n       <i>\n        CNN\n       </i>\n       reported the number of missing people to be about 117.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CNNOct14_141-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CNNOct14-141">\n         [141]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In a message to the DHS, Representatives\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nydia_Velazquez" title="Nydia Velazquez">\n        Nydia Velazquez\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Bennie_Thompson" title="Bennie Thompson">\n        Bennie Thompson\n       </a>\n       wrote, "It would be morally reprehensible to intentionally undereport the true death toll to portray relief efforts as more successful than they are."\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-VoxOct11_218-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-VoxOct11-218">\n         [218]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Between September\xc2\xa020 and October\xc2\xa018, the island\'s only medical examiner authorized 911\xc2\xa0bodies for cremation. The cause of death for the persons are listed as "natural causes", however.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-219">\n        <a href="#cite_note-219">\n         [219]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On November 3, 2017, San Yuan Mayor Yul\xc3\xadn Cruz said that the actual death toll for Puerto Rico may be as high as 500, which is more than 10 times higher than the current official death toll, as of early November 2017.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-10_times_higher_1-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-10_times_higher-1">\n         [1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Whitefish_Energy">\n        Whitefish Energy\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Maria&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Whitefish Energy">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:312px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Puerto_Rico_at_night_before_and_after_Hurricane_Maria.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="512" data-file-width="1024" height="155" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/86/Puerto_Rico_at_night_before_and_after_Hurricane_Maria.jpg/310px-Puerto_Rico_at_night_before_and_after_Hurricane_Maria.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/86/Puerto_Rico_at_night_before_and_after_Hurricane_Maria.jpg/465px-Puerto_Rico_at_night_before_and_after_Hurricane_Maria.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/86/Puerto_Rico_at_night_before_and_after_Hurricane_Maria.jpg/620px-Puerto_Rico_at_night_before_and_after_Hurricane_Maria.jpg 2x" width="310"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Puerto_Rico_at_night_before_and_after_Hurricane_Maria.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Comparison of lights at night in Puerto Rico before\n         <i>\n          (top)\n         </i>\n         and after\n         <i>\n          (bottom)\n         </i>\n         Hurricane Maria. Note: Lower image date should read September 25, 2017\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Soon after the hurricane struck,\n       <a href="/wiki/Whitefish_Energy" title="Whitefish Energy">\n        Whitefish Energy\n       </a>\n       \xe2\x80\x94a small Montana-based company with only two full-time employees\xe2\x80\x94was awarded a $300\xc2\xa0million contract by PREPA to repair Puerto Rico\'s power grid. The company contracted more than 300\xc2\xa0personnel and sent them to the island to carry out work. PREPA cited Whitefish\'s comparatively small upfront cost of $3.7\xc2\xa0million for mobilization as one of the main reasons for contracting them over larger companies. PREPA Executive Director Ricardo Ramos stated: "Whitefish was the only company -- it was the first that could be mobilized to Puerto Rico. It did not ask us to be paid soon or a guarantee to pay".\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Whitefish_ABC_220-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Whitefish_ABC-220">\n         [220]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       No requests for assistance were made to the\n       <a href="/wiki/American_Public_Power_Association" title="American Public Power Association">\n        American Public Power Association\n       </a>\n       by October\xc2\xa024.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Whitefish_ABC_220-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Whitefish_ABC-220">\n         [220]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The decision to hire such a tiny company was considered highly unusual by many, such as former Energy Department official Susan Tierney, who stated: "The fact that there are so many utilities with experience in this and a huge track record of helping each other out, it is at least odd why [the utility] would go to Whitefish\xe2\x80\x9d. As the company was based in Whitefish, Mont., the hometown of US Interior Secretary Ryan Zinke, this also led to accusations of privatization, though Zinke dismissed these claims and stated that he had no role in securing the contract.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-221">\n        <a href="#cite_note-221">\n         [221]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Several representatives, both Democrats and Republicans, also voiced their concern over the choice to contract Whitefish instead of other companies.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Whitefish_ABC_220-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Whitefish_ABC-220">\n         [220]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In a press release on October\xc2\xa027, FEMA stated it did not approve of PREPA\'s contract with Whitefish and cited "significant concerns".\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-222">\n        <a href="#cite_note-222">\n         [222]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Governor Rossell\xc3\xb3 subsequently ordered an audit of the contract\'s budget.\n       <a href="/wiki/Department_of_Homeland_Security_Office_of_Inspector_General" title="Department of Homeland Security Office of Inspector General">\n        DHS Inspector General\n       </a>\n       John Roth led the FEMA audit while Governor Rossell\xc3\xb3 called for a second review by Puerto Rico\'s Office of Management and Budget.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-223">\n        <a href="#cite_note-223">\n         [223]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       On October 29, PREPA cancelled the Whitefish contract after the governor demanded it.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-224">\n        <a href="#cite_note-224">\n         [224]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="U.S._Virgin_Islands">\n        U.S. Virgin Islands\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Maria&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: U.S. Virgin Islands">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       As of September 25, the U.S. Coast Guard reports that the ports of Crown Bay, East Gregerie Channel, West Gregerie Channel, and Redhook Bay on\n       <a href="/wiki/Saint_Thomas,_U.S._Virgin_Islands" title="Saint Thomas, U.S. Virgin Islands">\n        Saint Thomas\n       </a>\n       ; the ports of Krause Lagoon, Limetree Bay, and Frederiksted on\n       <a href="/wiki/Saint_Croix,_U.S._Virgin_Islands" title="Saint Croix, U.S. Virgin Islands">\n        Saint Croix\n       </a>\n       , and the port of Cruz Bay on\n       <a href="/wiki/Saint_John,_U.S._Virgin_Islands" title="Saint John, U.S. Virgin Islands">\n        Saint John\n       </a>\n       are open with restrictions.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FemaNewsSep25_180-6">\n        <a href="#cite_note-FemaNewsSep25-180">\n         [180]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On September 25, 11 flights arrived with 200,000 meals, 144,000 liters of water, and tarps.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FemaNewsSep25_180-7">\n        <a href="#cite_note-FemaNewsSep25-180">\n         [180]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Troops have been activated and deployed to the U.S. Virgin Islands from the\n       <a href="/wiki/Virginia_National_Guard" title="Virginia National Guard">\n        Virginia National Guard\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-225">\n        <a href="#cite_note-225">\n         [225]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       the\n       <a href="/wiki/West_Virginia_National_Guard" title="West Virginia National Guard">\n        West Virginia National Guard\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-226">\n        <a href="#cite_note-226">\n         [226]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Missouri_National_Guard" title="Missouri National Guard">\n        Missouri National Guard\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-227">\n        <a href="#cite_note-227">\n         [227]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       , and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UH-60_Blackhawk" title="UH-60 Blackhawk">\n        UH-60 Blackhawk\n       </a>\n       helicopters from the Tennessee Army National Guard.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Nearly a month after the hurricane, only 16 percent of people in St. Thomas and 1.6 percent of people in St. Croix have had electricity restored.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-228">\n        <a href="#cite_note-228">\n         [228]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Criticism_of_U.S._government_response">\n        Criticism of U.S. government response\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Maria&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Criticism of U.S. government response">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Carmenyulin.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2340" data-file-width="1761" height="266" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/99/Carmenyulin.jpg/200px-Carmenyulin.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/99/Carmenyulin.jpg/300px-Carmenyulin.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/99/Carmenyulin.jpg/400px-Carmenyulin.jpg 2x" width="200"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Carmenyulin.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         San Juan Mayor\n         <a href="/wiki/Carmen_Yul%C3%ADn_Cruz" title="Carmen Yul\xc3\xadn Cruz">\n          Carmen Yul\xc3\xadn Cruz\n         </a>\n         <i>\n          (pictured)\n         </i>\n         harshly criticized the federal response to Maria in Puerto Rico as inadequate.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The U.S. Department of Homeland Security (DHS) did not immediately waive the\n       <a href="/wiki/Merchant_Marine_Act_of_1920" title="Merchant Marine Act of 1920">\n        Jones Act\n       </a>\n       for Puerto Rico, which prevented the commonwealth from receiving any aid and supplies from non-U.S.-flagged vessels from U.S. ports.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-229">\n        <a href="#cite_note-229">\n         [229]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The waiver was granted after two days, while in contrast the waiver was not granted for\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Harvey" title="Hurricane Harvey">\n        Hurricane Harvey\n       </a>\n       until fourteen days after the hurricane and was narrowly drafted to only allow fuel transportation for seven days.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-230">\n        <a href="#cite_note-230">\n         [230]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       A DHS Security spokesman said that there would be enough U.S. shipping for Puerto Rico, and that the limiting factors would be port capacity and local transport capacity.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-auto1_231-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-auto1-231">\n         [231]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-auto1_231-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-auto1-231">\n         [231]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Guardian_0926_232-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Guardian_0926-232">\n         [232]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-233">\n        <a href="#cite_note-233">\n         [233]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       This statement was supported by AFL/CIO which issued a "fact checking" statement regarding the Jones Act and its effect upon recovery relief.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-234">\n        <a href="#cite_note-234">\n         [234]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The Jones Act was waived for a period of ten days starting on September 28 following a formal request by Puerto Rico Governor Rossell\xc3\xb3.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CBS_Jones_235-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CBS_Jones-235">\n         [235]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       San Juan Mayor\n       <a href="/wiki/Carmen_Yul%C3%ADn_Cruz" title="Carmen Yul\xc3\xadn Cruz">\n        Carmen Yul\xc3\xadn Cruz\n       </a>\n       , called the disaster a "terrifying humanitarian crisis" and pleaded for relief efforts to be sped up on September 26.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CruzQuote_236-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CruzQuote-236">\n         [236]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/White_House" title="White House">\n        White House\n       </a>\n       contested claims that the administration was not responding effectively.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BBC_0926_237-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-BBC_0926-237">\n         [237]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       General\n       <a href="/wiki/Joseph_L._Lengyel" title="Joseph L. Lengyel">\n        Joseph L. Lengyel\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Chief_of_the_National_Guard_Bureau" title="Chief of the National Guard Bureau">\n        Chief of the National Guard Bureau\n       </a>\n       , defended the Trump Administration\'s response, and reiterated that relief efforts were hampered by Puerto Rico being an island rather than on the mainland.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-238">\n        <a href="#cite_note-238">\n         [238]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       President\n       <a href="/wiki/Donald_Trump" title="Donald Trump">\n        Donald Trump\n       </a>\n       responded to accusations that he does not care about Puerto Rico: "Puerto Rico is very important to me, and Puerto Rico -- the people are fantastic people. I grew up in New York, so I know many people from Puerto Rico. I know many Puerto Ricans. And these are great people, and we have to help them. The island is devastated."\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-239">\n        <a href="#cite_note-239">\n         [239]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Frustrated with the federal government\'s "slow and inadequate response", relief group\n       <a href="/wiki/Oxfam" title="Oxfam">\n        Oxfam\n       </a>\n       announced on October 2 that it plans to get involved in the humanitarian aid effort, sending a team to "assess a targeted and effective response" and support its local partners\' on-the-ground efforts.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-240">\n        <a href="#cite_note-240">\n         [240]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       On October 2, 2017,\n       <a href="/wiki/Oxfam" title="Oxfam">\n        Oxfam\n       </a>\n       released a rare statement; "While the US government is engaged in relief efforts, it has failed to address the most urgent needs. Oxfam has monitored the response in Puerto Rico closely, and we are outraged at the slow and inadequate response the US Government has mounted,\xe2\x80\x9d said Oxfam America\xe2\x80\x99s president Abby Maxman. \xe2\x80\x9cOxfam rarely responds to humanitarian emergencies in the US and other wealthy countries, but as the situation in Puerto Rico worsens and the federal government\xe2\x80\x99s response continues to falter, we have decided to step in. The US has more than enough resources to mobilize an emergency response, but has failed to do so in a swift and robust manner.\xe2\x80\x9d\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-241">\n        <a href="#cite_note-241">\n         [241]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In an update on October\xc2\xa019, the agency called the situation in Puerto Rico "unacceptable" and called for "a more robust and efficient response from the US government".\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-OxfamOct19_242-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-OxfamOct19-242">\n         [242]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Puerto_Rico_Rally_IMG_7743_(37439192926).jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3456" data-file-width="5184" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Puerto_Rico_Rally_IMG_7743_%2837439192926%29.jpg/220px-Puerto_Rico_Rally_IMG_7743_%2837439192926%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Puerto_Rico_Rally_IMG_7743_%2837439192926%29.jpg/330px-Puerto_Rico_Rally_IMG_7743_%2837439192926%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Puerto_Rico_Rally_IMG_7743_%2837439192926%29.jpg/440px-Puerto_Rico_Rally_IMG_7743_%2837439192926%29.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Puerto_Rico_Rally_IMG_7743_(37439192926).jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         A rally for victims of the hurricane and Puerto Rico\'s status in general took place in\n         <a href="/wiki/Long_Beach,_California" title="Long Beach, California">\n          Long Beach, California\n         </a>\n         on October\xc2\xa03\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       On October 3, 2017, President Trump visited Puerto Rico. He compared the damage from Hurricane Maria to that of\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Katrina" title="Hurricane Katrina">\n        Hurricane Katrina\n       </a>\n       , saying: "If you looked \xe2\x80\x94 every death is a horror, but if you look at a real catastrophe like Katrina, and you look at the tremendous hundreds and hundreds and hundreds of people that died, and you look at what happened here with really a storm that was just totally overbearing, nobody has seen anything like this (...) What is your death count as of this morning, 17?".\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-243">\n        <a href="#cite_note-243">\n         [243]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Trump\'s remarks were widely criticized for implying that Hurricane Maria was not a "real catastrophe".\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-244">\n        <a href="#cite_note-244">\n         [244]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-245">\n        <a href="#cite_note-245">\n         [245]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       While in Puerto Rico, Trump also distributed canned goods and paper towels to crowds gathered at a relief shelter\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-246">\n        <a href="#cite_note-246">\n         [246]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and told the residents of the devastated island "I hate to tell you, Puerto Rico, but you\'ve thrown our budget a little out of whack, because we\'ve spent a lot of money on Puerto Rico, and that\'s fine. We saved a lot of lives."\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-247">\n        <a href="#cite_note-247">\n         [247]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       On October 12, Trump tweeted, "We cannot keep FEMA, the Military &amp; the First Responders, who have been amazing (under the most difficult circumstances) in P.R. forever!",\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Chicago-aid_248-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Chicago-aid-248">\n         [248]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       prompting further criticism from lawmakers in both parties\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WaPo-backlash_249-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-WaPo-backlash-249">\n         [249]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       ; Mayor Cruz replied, "You are incapable of empathy and frankly simply cannot get the job done."\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Guardian-hints_207-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Guardian-hints-207">\n         [207]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In response to a request for clarification on the tweet from Governor Rossell\xc3\xb3,\n       <a href="/wiki/John_F._Kelly" title="John F. Kelly">\n        John F. Kelly\n       </a>\n       assured that no resources were being pulled and replied: "Our country will stand with those American citizens in Puerto Rico until the job is done".\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NYT_Oct12_250-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NYT_Oct12-250">\n         [250]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      Hurricane Jose\n        </a>\n        in 2017 \xe2\x80\x93 major hurricane that passed dangerously close to some of the same areas affected by Hurricanes\n        <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Irma" title="Hurricane Irma">\n         Irma\n        </a>\n        and Maria.\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_David" title="Hurricane David">\n         Hurricane David\n        </a>\n        in 1979 \xe2\x80\x93 one of the deadliest tropical cyclones to hit Dominica\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Tropical_Storm_Erika" title="Tropical Storm Erika">\n         Tropical Storm Erika\n        </a>\n        in 2015 \xe2\x80\x93 devastated the island of Dominica with severe flooding\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Georges" title="Hurricane Georges">\n         Hurricane Georges\n        </a>\n        in 1998 \xe2\x80\x93 the last major hurricane to strike Puerto Rico\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Hugo" title="Hurricane Hugo">\n         Hurricane Hugo\n        </a>\n        in 1989 \xe2\x80\x93 the last Category\xc2\xa04 hurricane to strike Saint Croix\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Luis" title="Hurricane Luis">\n         Hurricane Luis\n        </a>\n        in 1995 \xe2\x80\x93 brought severe damage to several islands of the Lesser Antilles\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Marilyn" title="Hurricane Marilyn">\n         Hurricane Marilyn\n        </a>\n        in 1995 \xe2\x80\x93 affected Dominica and Guadeloupe and brought severe damage to the U.S. Virgin Islands\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Hortense" title="Hurricane Hortense">\n         Hurricane Hortense\n        </a>\n        in 1996 \xe2\x80\x93 affected Puerto Rico and caused widespread flooding across the island\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/1932_San_Ciprian_hurricane" title="1932 San Ciprian hurricane">\n         1932 San Ciprian hurricane\n        </a>\n        \xe2\x80\x93 last hurricane to make landfall in Puerto Rico at Category 4 strength or higher.\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="References">\n        References\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n times higher than reported"\n           </a>\n           <span class="reference-accessdate">\n            .
